Important News

Japan's Finances After the September 18th Incident 72

Tokyo Correspondence: Huai Ren

Time passes quickly, and the second anniversary of September 18th is approaching. Recalling the story of the Japanese army shelling the Beida Camp one night is like yesterday. In this fleeting year, Japan has obviously and substantially obtained the right to govern the three northeastern provinces. People of the yellow-uniformed class have, as they wished, strolled between the Black Water and White Mountains, singing their "Kimi ga Yo" song. But what about the other side of the coin? Obviously, there are very clear financial cracks on the three islands. Although we cannot say that these cracks are a harbinger of the empire's collapse, at least in the depths of these cracks, there seems to be a terrifying element.

Budget Implemented in Showa 7 (This Year)

Revenue Yuan

Regular Section 1,281,940,000

Temporary Section 498,468,000

Ordinary Revenue 45,096,000

Reserve Fund 453,372,000

Total 1,780,408,000

Expenditure Yuan

Regular Section 1,205,680,000

Temporary Section 574,728,000

Total 1,780,408,000

In this revenue budget of 1,780,408,000 yuan, 453,372,000 yuan from the reserve fund, accounting for more than one-quarter of the total revenue. The amount of more than 400 million yuan of public debt raised is indeed a very alarming figure. But this is not all. There is also 76,179,000 yuan of public debt in the special account section. In total, the amount of public debt issued by Japan this year will be 529,551,000 yuan. This flood of public debt is indeed a material worth noting in the recent financial history of Japan.

Now let's further examine the contents of this huge public debt amount:

General Account Yuan

Manchurian Incident Expenses Public Debt 249,045,000

Deficit Public Debt 160,546,000

Various Project Public Debt 43,780,000

Total 453,372,000

Special Account Project Public Debt Manchurian Incident Expenses Public Debt

Yuan

Governor-General of Korea 19,240,000 334,000

Governor-General of Taiwan 3,000,000

Kwantung Government 600,000 3,005,000

Sakhalin Government 1,000,000

Railway Special Account 49,000,000

Total 72,840,000 3,339,000

Total of General Account and Special Account 529,551,000

This statistical table clearly tells us that the interior of the more than 500 million yuan of public debt includes 252,384,000 yuan of Manchurian Incident expenses. In other words, one-half of Japan's financial difficulty this year is due to the September 18th Incident. From January to May of this year, in fact, 291,849,675 yuan of public debt has already been issued, including 113,371,550 yuan of Manchurian Incident expenses public debt, accounting for about one-half of the planned issue amount (to be continued)

Soviet Russia Withdraws Consulates from Northern Manchuria 73

 Soviet Banks and Companies Also Close Down

More Than 80,000 Red Army Troops Deployed Around Manchuli

The Reason is the Puppet State's Forcible Takeover of the Docks in the Eight Districts

Japanese Troops are Also Preparing to Send Troops to Boketu

Black Dragon River Correspondence: Soviet consuls stationed in various parts of Northern Manchuria, under orders from the Moscow government, will all lower their flags and return to their country within the next week. The Deputy Consul in Harbin, Rasiman, and the Consul in Dalian, Island Stezki, returned home on the 17th. The Soviet Far East Bank in Harbin has also been ordered to expedite its closure and await further instructions to cease operations. Yesterday, the bank transferred important documents and cash to the American Citibank for safekeeping. Some employees plan to return home around the 24th. The Soviet Far East Grain and Stone Trading Company and the Overseas Trading Company are also planning to close down within the next week. At the same time, the number of Soviet troops stationed inside and outside Manchuli has recently increased to more than 80,000. From Station No. 87 to Ulan-Ude, east to Abagaitu, and west to the shores of Lake Baikal, the Red Army is densely deployed, displaying their armor and conducting artillery and air combat exercises. On the 17th and 18th, more than 20 heavy artillery and aircraft conducted exercises in the skies over the Abagaitu border, conducting bombing and strafing exercises. Several hundred shells were fired each day, and the sound could be heard for more than ten miles. Houses in the area between Manchuli and Zhalantun were shaken. Due to the tense situation, merchants and residents closed their businesses, packed their furniture, and moved to Harbin and Heihe. Rumors are rampant between Hailar and Boketu. Merchants and residents along the western line of the East China Railway are moving to Harbin one after another, presenting a situation similar to that before the war. The reason for this change in attitude by Soviet Russia is the seizure of the docks in the Eight Districts of the Jiangbin area by the puppet Jiangyun Office. The resentment accumulated for more than ten months is about to be vented in one day. Therefore, the docks in the Eight Districts have become the fuse for the recent breakdown in relations between Japan and Russia. Last week, Sugihara, the Japanese Director of the General Affairs Department of the Puppet Northern Manchurian Negotiation Office, returned from Changchun and replied in writing to the Russian consulate in Harbin, explaining the takeover of the docks in the Eight Districts. However, the Russian consul refused to accept his note. The puppet office sent it three times, but it was rejected each time, and it declared that it would terminate direct negotiations with Manchuria from now on, clearly indicating its refusal to recognize the puppet state. On the Japanese side, preparations are being made to withdraw troops to the western line, intending to first hold the key points of the Xing'an Mountains, Hailar, Mian Duhe, and Boketu, and defend the area based on the terrain. On the other hand, it incited the puppet state to make concessions on the issue of the takeover of the docks in the Eight Districts, allowing the East China Railway to continue to sign leases, and canceling the double taxation on Russian imports at the Manchuli sub-customs, and handling it in accordance with the treaty signed between Nanjing and Soviet Russia. However, since Soviet Russia has already changed its attitude and has a definite foreign policy, it is no longer possible for the Japanese side to use the puppet state to ease its momentum. Two days ago, the Russian Consul-General in Harbin, Silausky, visited Zhang Jinghui, the Chief Executive of the Puppet Special District, and asked whether he was still under the orders of the Chinese government regarding the takeover of the docks in the Eight Districts and whether he was prepared to negotiate. If Zhang was still a Chinese official, Soviet Russia would begin negotiations with him on this matter. Zhang could not answer, and his Japanese advisor, Arai, responded on his behalf, answering that the matter was a diplomatic issue and could be handled directly with the negotiators. The Russian consul left displeased. On the 16th, more than 50 bandits hijacked the third passenger train from Harbin to Manchuli at the Boketu Yalu station on the Harbin-Manchuli line, killing seven railway protection soldiers and wounding more than ten soldiers and passengers. They left without looting. Afterwards, some said that it was the Japanese side using White Russians to disrupt the Harbin-Manchuli line, using the excuse that traffic was obstructed to send troops to protect it. This saying has gradually been confirmed in recent days, because the Japanese side has publicized this matter greatly and is preparing to send the 10th Division to Boketu first. (20th)

On the Jinzhou-Chaoyang Line 74

The Japanese Side Continues to Reinforce Troops

The Japanese Side Insists on Extending the Railway to Beipiao

Japanese Troops from Shenyang Are Also Heading West

Beijing Correspondence: The situation in Rehe has eased in recent days. At 7 pm on the 21st, a phone call came from Chengde, reporting that the local area was as calm as usual. The Rehe army is still stationed in Nanling. After negotiations between representatives and the Japanese army, both sides agreed not to attack each other and to cease military operations. The Rehe side is responsible for finding the whereabouts of Kwon Shiro Ishimoto. The Japanese troops stationed in the Chaoyangsi unit were still stationed near the station defense area on the afternoon of the 20th. The Jinzhou-Chaoyang branch line has been opened to traffic. According to news from Chaoyang, the Japanese troops stationed in Chaoyangsi are preparing to retreat. This proves that there is indeed a possibility of easing tensions. When the incident occurred, the Japanese army used the Ishimoto incident as an excuse to advance and clashed with the Zhang camp stationed in Chaoyangsi. At that time, our garrison withdrew to Nanling, which is a vital position, because it had not received orders. Nanling is a station on the Chaoyang line, with a tunnel passing through the ridge. Our army destroyed the tunnel to prevent the Japanese armored vehicles from advancing, so the Japanese army could not advance further west. Chaoyangsi is the border between Rehe and Liaoning, 20 miles from Yixian, 90 miles from Chaoyang, and 90 miles from Beipiao. Nanling is 8 miles from Chaoyangsi. After the situation eased, the Japanese troops in Chaoyangsi withdrew to Yixian, but a few remained in Chaoyangsi. Regarding the Ishimoto incident, which the Japanese used as an excuse, Ishimoto did not notify the local authorities when he entered the country, and our side did not know that he had entered the country. Since the Japanese side said that he was missing, in terms of friendship, our side could also help to find him. However, the Japanese Chief of Staff Yoshioka is very familiar with the strong resistance of the residents of Rehe and it is not easy to compromise, so the incident has eased. However, the Japanese side is determined to extend the Jinzhou-Chaoyang railway to Beipiao.

According to people from Rehe, the Rehe provincial authorities have sent a letter to the Japanese side, questioning why the Japanese used the excuse that Ishimoto was kidnapped by bandits to attack the Rehe border. If Ishimoto was really kidnapped by bandits, the Rehe authorities could have helped to find him if they had been notified by the Japanese side in advance. They could not attack because a person was missing, causing a military conflict. It is said that after receiving the letter, the Japanese side withdrew its troops and there have been no unexpected actions to date. Now both sides are trying to find Ishimoto's whereabouts. According to one version, the Japanese army is still continuing to reinforce troops on the Jinzhou-Chaoyang line, and the future is not optimistic. According to news received on the 22nd, Chengde is still peaceful. Our garrison is at the forefront in the Nanling-Beipiao area, while the Japanese troops are stationed in Yixian and Chaoyangsi. After negotiations between the two sides in recent days, (1) both sides ceased military operations; (2) Kwon Shiro Ishimoto's whereabouts will be investigated clearly before a rescue is attempted. According to intelligence from Shenyang, Japanese troops are continuing to move west towards Liaoxi, and their purpose is unknown. It is feared that they are still paying attention to Rehe. The volunteer army near Yixian is lurking in the deep mountains and forests, occasionally ambushing the Japanese army's rear. The Japanese army is often trapped by the volunteer army because the mountain roads are rugged and the terrain is unfamiliar. Therefore, the Japanese army does not dare to advance. (23rd)

The Volunteer Army 75

Plots to Seize Shenyang

Zhu Rongji's Plan Fails and He is Arrested

Shenyang Correspondence: Zhu Rongji (41 years old), the leader of the volunteer army in Liaoxi, was a former subordinate of Zhang Xueliang. Since the loss of the Northeast, Zhu was pained by the national crisis, so he gathered the volunteer army to operate in the counties west of Liaoning. In January and February of this year, he had the ambition to recover Shenyang. He sent 600 subordinates to sneak into Shenyang from Liuhezi. Zhu also personally accompanied Chief of Staff Ge Zonghai (43 years old) and Staff Zhu Changjiu (27 years old) to Shenyang to secretly investigate the security situation of Japan and the puppet state. He also purchased a large number of military supplies from Japanese ronin in Shenyang, planning to lead 600 volunteer soldiers to launch a night attack in Shenyang on the 7th of this month. Outside the city, Wang Zhichao and Liu Haiquan would lead the majority of the volunteer army to attack in coordination. Unfortunately, the Japanese army detected the plan in advance, and Zhu and the other two were arrested one after another. Therefore, on the night of the 7th, the volunteer army led by Wang and Liu launched a fierce attack on Liaoyang City from outside the city, but because there was no response from within, they retreated without winning. (July 21st)

Marine Corps Goes to Fujian 76

Chen Jitang Has Sent a Guard Brigade to Take Over

Chen Ce's Fleet is Divided

Establish a Pacification Office and Abolish the Qiongya Special District

Wu Chaoshu Advocates Limiting the Number of Troops Stationed in Qiongya

Guangzhou Correspondence: The conflict between the two Chens has come to an end after the mediation of Cai Tingkai and others. Before going to Fujian, Cai Tingkai sent Tan Qixiu, a brigade commander of the 19th Route Army, and Weng Guiqing, personnel from the rear of the route army, to Qiongya to handle the Marine Corps' departure to Fujian. On the 15th, Tan telegraphed Chen Ce from Qiongya, stating that he had arrived in Qiongya on the evening of the 14th and had decided to leave Qiongya with Chen Ji (commander of the Marine Corps regiment) and all the officers on the 19th, and that he had telegraphed Chen Zhangfu to lead the team to cross over to Qiongya to take over the defense. He was afraid that there would not be enough ships, so he asked to transfer the Fuan warship to Qiongya. After receiving the telegram, Chen Ce ordered Wu Zili, the captain of the Fuan warship, to go to Qiongya from Hong Kong on the 16th to pick up the Marine Corps stationed in Qiongya to go to Fujian. After Tan Qixiu had inspected all the regiments of the Marine Corps in Qiongya, he ordered the Marine Corps' 4th Regiment, led by Li Hansheng, to set off on a merchant ship on the 18th. The remaining 1st, 2nd, and 3rd Regiments also disembarked on the 18th. According to Chen Ce, the Marine Corps' trip to Fujian was not a reorganization. It would still use the name of the Marine Corps to cooperate with the 19th Route Army to suppress bandits. As for the fleet, such as Zhongshan, Fuan, Hairui, etc., were still under his command, while the six shallow-water warships that could not go to sea, which were currently berthed in Hong Kong, were handed back to the Guangdong Provincial Government for management. As for Chen Jitang, since Chen Ce's troops had left Qiongya one after another, he ordered Chen Zhangfu, a member of the Southern Route Pacification Committee, to send a team to Qiongya to take over the defense. After receiving the order, Chen drew from Leizhou Chen Hanguang's guard brigade, He Baoshu's 2nd Regiment, and Peng Zhifang's 3rd Regiment, and sent them to Haikou. Chen Hanguang led Chen Yuguang's 1st Regiment to Qiongya on the 18th, and set up a brigade headquarters in Haikou. Chen Zhangfu also decided to go to Qiongya within a few days to inspect everything. As for the six ships stationed in Hong Kong, Jiang, Jiang Da, Zhixin, Pingxi, Hushan, and Xixing, Chen Jitang has sent personnel to Hong Kong to discuss the takeover, so that they can return to the province.

Regarding the aftermath of Qiongya, on the 16th, the Southwest Political Affairs Committee also ordered the Guangdong Provincial Government that all the people's wealth, politics, and all construction matters in Qiongya should be earnestly taken care of by the provincial government. After receiving the order, the provincial government ordered the former county magistrates of Qiongya who had left their posts to return to their counties by the 25th of this month, otherwise they would be considered to have abandoned their posts. As for the pacification of the local area, the Southwest Political Affairs Committee separately ordered the First Group Army to set up a Qiongya Pacification Office to handle everything. It is said that after the Pacification Office is established, the Qiongya Special District plan may be cancelled. Recently, the Southwest Political Affairs Committee has discussed this issue, because someone has petitioned the government to abolish the Qiongya Special District system, and some have attacked Wu Chaoshu, the chief of the Qiongya Special District, because of this Qiongya affair. However, Wu still sent a letter to Chen Jitang in the name of the chief of the special district, requesting to limit the number of troops taking over Qiongya, fearing that although the Qiongya military affairs will be resolved in the future, there will still be some political waves, because one side wants to abolish the Qiongya Special District system, while the other side wants to maintain the original plan, and their political views are still not fully in line. The following is an excerpt from Wu's letter to Chen, so as to clarify Wu's political views on governing Qiongya: "As the nominal chief of the Qiongya district, I have given some thought to the cooperative method between the special district government and your group army's (referring to the First Group Army) troops stationed in Qiongya in the future. I have found that when the banditry in Qiongya was rampant in 1928, Chief Ye Zhaozhao of your unit only led a regiment of troops to Haikou, divided into several routes to search and suppress, and was determined to drive them out. Within a few days, great results were achieved. To this day, the people of Qiongya still praise him, which shows that the success or failure of the army's suppression of bandits does not depend on the number of troops. Now the banditry in the Qiongya district is about the same as in 1928. I think that 1,500 to 2,000 troops stationed in Qiongya is enough. This is the first thing that should be discussed. Since this unit is specifically going to Qiongya to suppress bandits, the military pay required can be raised locally. However, the Qiongya district's monthly income is only more than 100,000 yuan, so there should be a certain limit to the supply of military pay, so as not to hinder other administrative facilities. It is proposed that the special district government raise 35,000 to 40,000 yuan in silver dollars per month. If there is a shortfall, your unit will still raise it. This is the second thing that should be discussed. On February 27 of this year, I reported to the Political Affairs Committee, stating that the Marine Corps currently stationed in the Qiongya district can be completely withdrawn when the banditry is slightly suppressed, and that there is no need for central troops to be stationed afterwards. However, the arrival of foreign troubles is difficult to predict. When necessary, the chief of the special district should report to the central government, or consult with nearby chiefs, to send land, sea, and air forces to protect it, so as to strengthen national defense, etc. Now the Qiongya District Government is established within a few days, and it is expected that the security team will be fully organized in about three months. At that time, it is proposed that the troops sent by your unit be withdrawn from Qiongya to comply with the original plan. This is the third thing that should be discussed. In short, your unit's trip to Qiongya to suppress bandits is very welcome. The above three points are purely based on facts, so that the military and political affairs and the people's wealth and politics can each be properly divided and conducive to implementation." Judging from Wu's letter, he not only asked Chen Jitang to limit the number of troops going to Qiongya, but also asked Chen's troops to withdraw if necessary. However, Chen Jitang wants to include Qiongya in his scope with the strength of a lion fighting a rabbit. It is unknown what answer he will give to Wu's request. (July 19th)

Guangdong Bandit Suppression Army 77

Reorganization of Two Columns

Xiang Hanping Goes to Nanxiong to Arrange Bandit Suppression

Guangzhou correspondence: Since the Guangdong army repelled the Communist bandits who attacked Nanxiong, it has recently been continuously increasing its troop strength on the border. However, it has not yet launched a large-scale encirclement because the main force of the Communist bandits is still in Xinfeng, while the remaining small number are still active in the San'nan area on the Jiangxi border, appearing as if they are waiting for an opportunity to invade the Guangdong border again. Therefore, Chen Jitang, for the sake of prudence, has telegraphed the Independent First Division under Huang Renhuan and the Independent Second Division under Zhang Ruigui, stationed in Dongjiang, to guard Xunwu, Lianping, and Heping on the Jiangxi border. The Eighth Division under Huang Zhiwen has also been ordered to suspend its return to the province and temporarily station in Xingning and Wuhua to assist in defending the northeastern border, awaiting further orders. As for the units in the Beijiang area, they are now organized into two columns. The first column is commanded by Yu Hanmou, and the second column is commanded by Xiang Hanping. However, news from Daju to Nanxiong is still not clear, and traffic above the Zhongzhan station in Nanxiong has not yet been restored. The Guangdong military authorities are currently building fortifications above Nanxiong. The Nanxiong airfield has been renovated and completed. Six aircraft from the Second Air Force Squadron and two from the Fourth Squadron have departed for Nanxiong to scout the bandit situation ahead. The Guangdong army in Nanxiong currently includes Li Hanun's Independent Third Division, Chen Zhangfu's Second Independent Brigade, Deng Longguang's Training Division, the four regiments of Zhang Da's unit of the Fifth Division of the Second Army, and the remnants of Zhang Meixin's Fourth Division, who retreated from Xinfeng, totaling about fifteen or sixteen regiments. All are under the command of Xiang Hanping, the commander of the Second Column. After receiving the order, Xiang departed for Shao on the 16th and arrived in Shaoguan at 5:00 PM that day. In Shao, he summoned officers of all ranks for a bandit suppression meeting to discuss and determine a plan for encircling and suppressing the Communist bandits. He telegraphed Chen Jitang in Guangzhou and Yu Hanmou in Daju, Chen Cheng in Ganzhou, He Jian in Hunan Province, and Mao Weishou on the Fujian border, in order to carry out a large-scale encirclement when the time comes. The next day, Xiang, accompanied by Chief of Staff Tan Da, flew to Nanxiong to inspect the troops and inspect the fortifications, and to discuss the pursuit and suppression with the officers in Nanxiong. Subsequently, as the local Communists above Nanxiong had not yet been wiped out, a special order was issued to the troops at the front to expedite the suppression. Therefore, on the 17th and 18th, the Chen Zhang Brigade and Zhang Da Division at the front attacked Dayuanli. More than a thousand bandits were eventually unable to hold out and retreated to Datangzhai. Government troops are still suppressing them. On the 19th, another order was issued to search and advance towards Xinfeng, with the fresh troops of Chen Hengjie's regiment taking the lead. As for the Guangxi army under Wang Zanbin, they concentrated in Juntian on the 20th and immediately departed for Shaoguan. It is heard that Commander Wang will go to the front on the 21st, and will also be under the command of Xiang Hanping. (July 21st)

Hunan Provincial Government Asks the Central Government 78

To Limit Troop Recruitment in Hunan

Changsha correspondence: In recent years, a large number of armies have come to Hunan Province to recruit soldiers, and in recent months, there has hardly been a day without recruiters coming to Hunan. Fearing that this would lead to malpractices, the Hunan Provincial Government has petitioned the Military Affairs Commission and consulted the Ministry of Military Affairs to order all armies to limit recruitment in Hunan. The text presented to the Military Affairs Commission is recorded below: "Your Excellency, the province previously, because the Communist bandits and local bandits have not been completely eliminated and are being closely suppressed, is deeply concerned that the various troops coming to Hunan to recruit soldiers and laborers will give the bandits and Communists in the counties an opportunity to infiltrate, causing endless harm to the army and the local area in the future. In May of the 18th year, we petitioned Your Excellency to order all armies not to recruit in Hunan again, and the order was approved on file. Subsequently, due to the urgent military situation of bandit suppression, when the armies in various places have vacancies, they still send personnel from time to time to contact us and ask for convenience. The Provincial Government believes that serving as a soldier is a citizen's duty and cannot be strictly rejected. We can only formulate measures that all those who come to Hunan to recruit must have an area designated by the Provincial Government to show restrictions, and at the same time notify the counties and military police agencies to take care of them. This kind of procedure is already very cumbersome. In recent years, personnel have been sent from various places to Hunan to recruit soldiers almost every day. Each county has recruitment offices, as many as a dozen. The reason why recruiters are concentrated here is simply because the people of Hunan are able to endure hardship and are easy to train. However, the harm suffered by the province is indescribable. Most of the recruits are farmers and workers who are healthy and strong, who can support themselves in their hometowns. Once someone recruits them, they think they can eat without farming and wear clothes without weaving. They abandon their original occupations and follow suit. Some who have been in the army for a long time become accustomed to the prosperity of the city. When they are demobilized or disbanded, they despise the rural life of the past, gather in cities, and become unemployed vagrants. They even privately hide firearms, collude with bandits, gather in the mountains and forests, and habitually rob. In recent years, most of the bandit cases solved everywhere are retired soldiers, which is clear evidence. Moreover, soldiers from Hunan Province account for the majority of the troops. In the event of casualties, the chief officers rarely care. All pensions are transferred by the Ministry of Military Affairs to Hunan Province for payment. Recently, the national and local taxes pay more than one million in pensions every year, which is a special expenditure not found in other provinces. Now, after the soldiers and bandits in the province, there is also a natural disaster. The strong are scattered in all directions, and laborers are recruited, making it difficult to cope. If recruitment continues like this and all the strong men are incorporated into the army, the fields will be barren and the industry will be in decline, which will affect the social economy and local security to a great extent. We propose that you observe the local situation and allow all armies not to send personnel to Hunan for recruitment in the future. If it is necessary to recruit in Hunan due to the actual needs, the number should be limited by each unit and reported to the Ministry of Military Affairs for approval, which will then be transferred to the Provincial Government for handling in accordance with the regulations to show caution. All the reasons for restricting recruitment in Hunan are reported to Your Excellency in addition to consulting the Ministry of Military Affairs, and we ask for your approval and instructions to be obeyed. Respectfully presented."

Anhui People Thoroughly Investigate Malpractices in Disaster Relief Work in Northern Anhui 79

Bengbu correspondence: After the representatives of the twenty-one counties in northern Anhui, who were receiving disaster relief, reported the case of provincial officials in charge of disaster relief and transportation personnel engaging in private corruption and delaying disaster relief work, the National Government's Relief Commission and the Control Yuan successively sent personnel to Bengbu to investigate. However, due to the failure to find conclusive evidence of corruption, the case could not be handed over to the court. The representatives of the twenty-one counties in northern Anhui, who were receiving disaster relief, believed that the investigators had failed to conduct a thorough investigation and expressed great dissatisfaction. They again petitioned the National Government's Relief Commission to send impartial personnel, together with representatives from the Anhui Fellow Association in Beijing and Shanghai, to form an investigation delegation to thoroughly investigate the truth of the malpractices. The National Government's Relief Commission specially sent Sun Yunsheng and Wang Chusheng, and the Anhui Fellow Association in Shanghai appointed Yue Xiangru and Lü Yin'nan, while the Anhui Fellow Association in Shanghai and Beijing appointed Shi Dechun and Wang Zhaoquan to jointly form an investigation delegation to conduct a thorough investigation. Sun and others arrived in Bengbu together a few days ago and conducted a detailed investigation into the various truths of the slow delivery of relief wheat, price changes into flour, reduced distribution quantities, late release of urgent needs, changes in distribution, appointment of private individuals, and embezzlement of relief funds. They also sought opinions from all parties to provide evidence. The members of the Post-Disaster Relief Association in northern Anhui specially held a meeting at Bamu Garden at 5:00 PM on the 20th to welcome the delegation. Shi Dechun and Wang Chusheng gave speeches, expressing their opinions on investigating the case, stating that they would conduct an impartial investigation and would never be lenient. Representatives from various counties gave extremely painful reports, especially criticizing Quan Shaowu, the Commissioner of Disaster Relief in Northern Anhui, for his sloppy work and delay in disaster relief. It is now known that Quan Shaowu has returned to his hometown of Beiping on the pretext of a poor environmental air, and various parties speculate that he has fled with embezzled funds. Whether this is true or not remains to be verified by the delegation's thorough investigation. (July 21st)

Suzhou 81

Record of the Court Hearing of the Ma Xu Lawsuit It is reported that Ma Baolin, a middle school student in Suzhou County, and Xu Caizhen, a female vocational student, an unmarried couple, both committed suicide by poisoning. Ma died from the poisoning, and Xu was saved after medical treatment. Afterwards, Xu, as an unmarried wife, requested to observe chastity for Ma, but Ma's family firmly refused, which led to a mutual fight between Xu Caizhen and Ma's stepmother, Zhang. Both were slightly injured. The two sides then hired lawyers to file a complaint with the local court. Zhang accused Xu Caizhen of trespassing and assault. The case was heard yesterday (25th). At 8:30 AM, Xu Caizhen and her mother, Xu Tang, arrived at the court. Many of Xu's relatives arrived, and the audience was extremely crowded. Those who arrived later had almost no place to stand. The court opened at 10:26 AM. Xu hired lawyer Ma Heng, and Ma's side hired three lawyers, Lu Hongyi, Zhou Yuong, and Gu Enpei, to appear in court for defense. As a result, it was ordered that the two sides try to reconcile outside the court. If reconciliation fails, the court will hold another hearing. The court will conduct an investigation and schedule a continued hearing, and then adjourned the court.

The Addition of Vehicle Permits Caused a Dispute The Wuxian Education Bureau previously owed a huge amount of 170,000 yuan in education fees. It agreed with the Construction Bureau to add 500 rickshaw permits, collecting a deposit of 160 yuan per permit, totaling 80,000 yuan, to pay the education fees. The added vehicle permits were distributed to the members of the Rickshaw Trade Association according to the number of vehicles they originally had. Unexpectedly, this aroused the opposition of non-members, who requested the Education Bureau and the Party Department for relief, demanding to be allocated the vehicle permits. The County Party Department convened talks between the two sides on the morning of the 25th and invited members of the Education and Construction Bureaus to attend. After a period of talks, there was no result. The various trade associations in Wuxian County have now submitted a request to the Construction Department for an explanation of whether non-members can enjoy the rights. It is difficult to resolve for the time being.

Shop Owner Rapes Teenage Girl Yu Yirong, who runs a salted fish shop on Hengjie Street outside Fengmen, has a maid, Zhang Maotou, who is 18 years old and quite beautiful. In March of this year, when Yu Yirong's wife returned to her mother's home, Yu Yirong took the opportunity to go to Zhang Maotou's room and raped Zhang Maotou by means of intimidation. Zhang Maotou's father heard about it and immediately ordered his daughter to quit her job and work for the Peng family on Shiquan Street. The day before yesterday, Yu sent a stranger, Zha Qiaomei, to the Peng family to persuade Zhang Maotou, saying that Yu intended to take Zhang Maotou as a concubine. Unexpectedly, the girl's father found out and twisted Yu and Zha to the police station in charge. After a brief interrogation, the case was transferred to the court for interrogation on the grounds that it involved the rape of a woman under the age of twenty.

Chongming 82

The Opening of the Bridge Town Plague Hospital Since the beginning of summer in this county, due to the hot weather, the plague has been rampant. Those who are infected die quickly in the morning and evening. If measures are not taken to prevent it, the future will be dangerous. The people of this port, in view of this, raised funds to open a temporary plague hospital. The Ning Shao Guild Hall in Zhonghua Bridge was chosen as the hospital site. Liu Fuchen was publicly elected as the hospital director. Since the 15th, the clinic has been opened first, and the number of people who come to the hospital for vaccinations every day is very crowded. Now the hospital has been set up and officially opened yesterday.

Kunshan 83

A Convict Tried to Escape by Climbing Over the Wall Fang Guilin, who had been sentenced to seven months in Kunshan County Prison, took advantage of the absence of the guard at 2:00 PM on the 24th, climbed over the roof to the prison wall, and descended from the power pole to escape. A police officer, Mr. Du, caught a glimpse of him and quickly chased after him. Near Xiaoximen, the convict saw that there was a river in front and jumped into the river. Du managed to capture the convict and sent him to the team headquarters. He was then sent to the prison to be shackled and imprisoned, and will be sent to the county government today for handling.

The Epidemic Prevention Center Has Opened This year, the tiger plague has been rampant in Kunshan County, spreading to various villages, and deaths have followed. Although doctors from various hospitals have injected vaccines in the city and countryside, it is not easy to popularize them, so the epidemic has not been slightly reduced. The authorities, in view of this, actively organized an epidemic prevention center, surveyed the Chen Family Ancestral Hall in Shanqian as the site, and appointed Qin Jieren as the director. After Qin's deployment, it opened yesterday, and Wang Hongxun and Wu Baode were invited to be doctors, as well as seven assistants and nurses. After the opening, people went to the clinic in an endless stream, which shows the rampant nature of the tiger plague in Kunshan.

Wuxi 84

Ruichangrun Accused of Embezzlement Ruichangrun Silk Cocoon Warehouse under Gongyun Bridge in this county has been established for many years and its business is quite good. It can be regarded as the leader in the industry. On the 9th of last month, Yichun Baoyu Cocoon Firm came to Wuxi to store 190 bales of dry cocoons in the warehouse. At that time, the cocoon bales were selected and weighed, and there was no difference in weight. When Baoyu Cocoon Firm went to pick up the goods on the 12th of this month, it suddenly found that the bale corners were moved. Each bale was 6 or 7 catties less, while the ten or so bales at the bottom were not moved, and the weight increased by a certain amount compared to the original weight. The manager of Baoyu Cocoon Firm, Yu Baosan, negotiated with Wu Buzhou, the manager of the warehouse. Because the conditions were not suitable, Yu Baosan filed a criminal lawsuit with the County Court Procuratorate, accusing the warehouse of embezzlement in its business. The day before yesterday, Prosecutor Shen opened a court hearing. As a result, the defendant was ordered to pay a written guarantee of 2,000 yuan to wait for investigation and handling.

The Township Head Leads the Crowd to Destroy a Small Wheel At Gongyun Bridge outside the North Gate, Yongji Small Wheel of the Shanglun Shipping Bureau, on the Yugi line, was sailing from Yugi to the city the day before yesterday. When passing the Luxiang area of Beihai Township in the 16th District, the township head of the township, Lu Bingzhang, led eight or ninety villagers, holding wooden sticks and other weapons, waiting under the bridge, and ordered the ship to stop. The driver, Chen Qiaoquan, had no choice but to stop the ship. Lu immediately led the villagers to board the ship, destroying the machinery and glass windows on the tugboat, and injuring the driver, Chen Qiaoquan, and two others. They dispersed in a crowd. Afterwards, Chen Qiaoquan and others went to the County Court to examine the injuries, and Shen Zhaotang, the manager of the bureau, reported to the County Public Security Bureau to send police to the countryside to arrest Lu and send him to the bureau. Today (25th), he will be transferred to the County Court for interrogation.

(4) The added long-distance telephones include the Xichang Line, the Xicheng Line, Changre County, and the Tongyang Line. Other matters include the establishment of urban and rural telephones in Songjiang, Chongming, Nanhui, Qidong, Rugao, and other counties, the recruitment of long-distance telephone students, and the addition of radio stations. (5)

Internal administration is especially important. In the past six months, reforms have been made to improve the receipt and dispatch of documents, the processing of documents and reports, the regulations on the Dianzhi method, the sorting of archives, and the investigation of the construction bureaus and administrative conditions of various counties.

Huzhou 87

Xiaoshu Town Goes on Strike The Xiaoshu Town, which belongs to Anji County in the western part of the city, has a Fuchang grocery store opened by Huang Meicai. On the 4th of this month, several sanitary policemen from Meixi Town came to the store and took out the salted meat stored in the pickling vat, falsely claiming that it was for sale, which hindered hygiene, and wanted to fine five yuan. The shop owner said that the meat was prepared for self-consumption and was not for sale, which led to a dispute between the two sides. After the town district chief asked the county government for instructions, he was fined six days of labor service in accordance with the regulations of the convention. Unexpectedly, Director Pan of the Bureau ordered six armed policemen to the town on the 20th and took the young owner of Fuchang away. On the 21st, he ordered another team of police with guns and ammunition to tie up the shop owner Huang Meicai and take him away. The whole city was in turmoil, arousing public outrage. Starting from the 22nd, all 200 or so shops in the town went on strike, and more than 500 citizens of the town volunteered to go to the county government to petition.

Chu Minyi and Chen Bijun Visit Scenic Spots Chu Minyi, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan, and Chen Bijun, wife of Wang Jingwei, arrived in Hangzhou at 9:14 PM on the 23rd with a floral car attached, and then took a car to visit the West Lake. An Underage Child Thief Was Arrested Xu Jinkui, a 16-year-old boy, used to work as a young orderly in a certain military camp. He was dismissed and became a vagrant in Hangzhou. It was difficult for him to make a living. He met Zhu Ziwen, an apprentice who had closed his business in Shengchang Garden in Xinxishi Market. He was 15 years old. The two felt sorry for each other and decided to rob. They stole a kitchen knife and sneaked to the railway outside Genshan Gate, waiting for passers-by to pass by, threatening them with knives and searching them. However, those who passed by here were all villagers, carrying at most one or two corners of foreign coins. Last night, a villager passed by and was robbed and ran away, shouting for arrest. The police officer chased and caught them. He was sent to the Hangzhou Local Court for interrogation on the grounds of robbery. He confessed to three robberies, totaling three corners of foreign coins and twenty-three copper coins, which were equally divided and used for living expenses. It was said that they were forced by life. It should be punished for daring to rob continuously in the outskirts of the provincial capital. He was prosecuted in accordance with the crime of banditry, but both were under the age of sixteen, and the crime was considered.

Strict Order to Suppress Dispersed Soldiers and Vagrants Bengbu is a key transportation hub connecting the north and south, and is a thoroughfare for the Huai River. Education News

Important News 90

Zhejiang University Changes Organization

Centralizing Administrative Power in the Secretariat

Military Training and Physical Education Departments Directly Under the President

Abolishing the Dean of Students Office, Replacing it with Student Life Counselors

Hangzhou News: Our reporter, because Zhejiang University President Cheng Tianfang recently returned to Hangzhou, especially went to inquire about the situation of his negotiations for funding in Beijing yesterday. Mr. Cheng received him and said that the presidents' meeting of colleges and universities decided on three measures regarding the funding issue and submitted them to the Executive Yuan, namely (1) full payment starting from July; (2) Promptly clear the arrears of this year; (3) In the future, educational funds must be designated as special funds, such as customs duties and Boxer Indemnity, etc. Later, President Wang formally replied, acknowledging that funding would no longer be in arrears starting from July and would not be discounted. The repayment of old debts was also acknowledged in principle, but the timing of repayment was not determined. As for the third item, the Executive Yuan did not agree. Mr. Cheng also expressed his opinions on the organizational changes of Zhejiang University, saying that since he came to Zhejiang University three months ago, the most peculiar thing he felt was that Zhejiang University had no complete organizational regulations in the past. The organization of each college was different from each other and extremely complicated. The documents, accounting affairs, student affairs, and libraries of each college were independent of each other and not subordinate to each other, with many shortcomings. For example, each college had to set up such staff, which was numerous, resulting in large salaries and a waste of resources. Each college acted on its own, which caused various difficulties in university administration. When the Secretariat had something to contact with the colleges, it had to use official documents, which was no different from the university dealing with external organizations. After I came to Zhejiang University, many teachers and students suggested reforms. This time, when I talked to Minister Zhu in Beijing, Minister Zhu also advocated reform. During the presidents' meeting, the presidents of various universities also advocated that the organization of universities should strive for simplicity. Therefore, I drafted more than 20 articles of Zhejiang University regulations in Beijing, referring to the established cases of other universities. Minister Zhu expressed deep sympathy, and the administrative meeting held today slightly revised and passed them, and they were implemented on the same day. The most important points of these regulations are: (1) Centralizing administrative power in the Secretariat, with the Secretary-General in charge, and setting up six sections: Documentation, Registration, Accounting, General Affairs, Library, and Publication, to handle university affairs. In the future, the deans of each college will only be responsible for teaching affairs and academic equipment, etc. According to this method, staff salaries and office expenses will definitely save a lot, and handling affairs can be faster than before, and it is no longer necessary to communicate with official documents; (2) The Department of Military Training and the Department of Physical Education are directly under the President, so that the entire school can receive unified military and physical education training; (3) Abolish the Dean of Students Office and replace it with student life counselors. National universities do not have a Dean of Students Office. The nature of student life counselors is to live with students and guide them into the right path. After Mr. Cheng finished talking, he presented a copy of the organizational regulations as a gift. They are recorded as follows:

Organizational Regulations of Zhejiang University

Chapter 1: General Principles, Article 1: This university is named National Zhejiang University. Article 2: This university is based on the educational purpose of the Republic of China and its implementation guidelines, with the purpose of promoting culture, researching academics, cultivating sound character, and cultivating specialized talents. Chapter 2: Academic System, Article 3: This university temporarily sets up the following colleges and departments: (1) College of Arts and Sciences, with departments of Literature, Politics, Education, Mathematics, Physics, Chemistry, Biology, etc.; (2) College of Engineering, with departments of Electrical Engineering, Mechanical Engineering, Chemical Engineering, Civil Engineering, etc.; (3) College of Agriculture, with departments of Agronomy, Forestry, Horticulture, Sericulture, Agricultural Society, etc. Article 4: The duration of study at this university is set at four years. After graduation, students can be called Bachelor of... Article 5: Entrusted by the Zhejiang Provincial Government, this university establishes advanced industrial secondary schools and advanced agricultural secondary schools, affiliated to the Colleges of Engineering and Agriculture. Their regulations will be determined separately. Chapter 3: Organizational System, Article 6: This university has one president, who has overall control of university affairs and is appointed by the National Government. Article 7: This university has one secretary-general, who is hired by the president and, with the president's approval, handles all university affairs. Article 8: Each college of this university has one dean, who is hired by the president and, with the president's approval, handles all teaching affairs and academic equipment matters of the college. Each college may have one vice-dean to assist in college affairs. Article 9: Each department of this university has one chairman, and several professors, associate professors, lecturers, and teaching assistants, who are hired by the dean with the president's approval. Article 10: Each factory, farm, and forest farm of this university may have one director and several technicians, who are hired by the president from among professors, associate professors, and lecturers, with the approval of the president and dean, to handle factory, farm, or forest farm affairs. Article 11: The factories, farms, forest farms, and experimental laboratories of each department of this university may have technicians, managers, or assistants, who are hired or appointed by the dean with the approval of the president. Article 12: This university has one or two secretaries, who assist the president and secretary-general in handling all university affairs. Article 13: The Secretariat of this university is divided into six sections: Documentation, Registration, Accounting, General Affairs, Library, and Publication. Each section has one director, who is hired by the president, and several staff members and assistants, who are appointed by the president, to handle the affairs of each section under the direction of the president and secretary-general. The detailed rules for the Secretariat and each section will be determined separately. Article 14: This university has a Department of Military Training, with one director and several instructors and teaching assistants, who are hired by the president to handle all military training matters of the university under the direction of the president. Article 15: This university has a Department of Physical Education, with one director and several lecturers and teaching assistants, who are hired by the president to handle all physical education matters of the university under the direction of the president. Article 16: This university has several student life counselors, who are hired by the president to guide students in their life on campus under the direction of the president. Article 17: This university has several school doctors, who are hired by the president, and three medical staff members, who are appointed by the president, to handle health and medical matters. Article 18: The Secretariat of this university has a typing room with several clerks, who are appointed by the president to handle typing matters. Chapter 4: Meetings, Article 19: This university has a university affairs meeting, which is composed of the president, secretary-general, deans of each college, chairmen of each department, and representatives of professors and associate professors. Article 20: The director of the Department of Military Training, the director of the Department of Physical Education, the secretaries of the Secretariat, the directors of each section, and the student life counselors may be invited by the president to attend the university affairs meeting. Article 21: Each college of this university has a college affairs meeting, which is composed of the dean, vice-dean, chairmen of each department, directors of each factory or farm, professors, and associate professors. Article 22: The Secretariat of this university has an administrative meeting, which is composed of the secretary-general, secretaries, and directors of each section. Article 23: The regulations for the university affairs meeting, college affairs meeting, and administrative meeting will be determined separately. Chapter 5: Committees, Article 24: This university has the following committees, whose members are hired by the president from among the university faculty and staff: (1) Admissions Committee; (2) Publications Committee; (3) Audit Committee; (4) Construction Committee; (5) Student Affairs Committee; (6) Health Committee; (7) Lecture Committee; (8) Academic Equipment Committee. Article 25: This university may establish other committees according to the needs of university affairs. Article 26: The regulations for each committee will be determined separately. Chapter 6: Supplementary Provisions, Article 27: These regulations will be implemented after being approved by the president and reported to the Ministry of Education for record. Article 28: If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, the president may revise them at any time and report them to the Ministry of Education for record.

Record of the Annual Meeting of the Chinese Testing Society

Reading of Testing Papers and Election of Directors

The Chinese Testing Society was initiated and organized by educational scholars and psychologists in the country. Cai Yuanpei and Dai Jitao, members of the Central Committee, are sponsors of the Society and have provided much assistance to the Society's affairs. Since its establishment in June of last year, all plans have been gradually implemented. The Testing Magazine published by the Society has recently reached its second issue, with rich content and detailed research, which is especially praised by the educational community. July of this year marks the anniversary of the Society's establishment, and the first annual meeting was held at Yenching University in Peiping this month. Registration was on the morning of the 15th, with more than 50 members and representatives. The opening ceremony was held at 3:00 p.m. on the afternoon of the 17th. Lu Zhiwei, director of the Department of Psychology at Yenching University, was elected as chairman. After reporting on the purpose of the meeting, Zhou Xuezhang, representative of Yenching University, delivered a welcome speech, extending a warm welcome to the members from Nanjing. Then, Long Yun, representative of the Central Party Headquarters, delivered a speech, praising the Society's research spirit and hoping for continued efforts, etc. The Board of Directors asked Ai Wei, professor at Central University, to report on the Society's affairs in the past year, and Yi Kejian to report on the economic situation in the past year. At 7:00 p.m., there was a tea party hosted by the members of Yenching University. During the party, Lu Zhiwei's performance on testing was quite unique. On the morning of the 18th, at 8:00 a.m., papers were read, including "The Theory, Method, and Implementation of Educational Diagnosis" by Du Yuanzai, professor at Peiping Normal University, "The Progress of Middle School Chinese Language Testing in the Past Five Years" by Professor Ai Wei, "A Comparative Study of Ethical Concepts between Two Ethnic Groups" by Professor Zhang Yi, and "The Process of Revising the Chinese Binet-Simon Test" by Wu Wenmin. Each of these papers contained the results of personal research, which were highly valued by the education and psychology communities. At 1:00 p.m., participants visited the Peiping Library and the Institute of Psychology of the Academia Sinica, and toured the Sanhai Park. A dinner party was held in the evening, with the participation of all the colleagues from the Institute of Psychology and Miss Li Mo, a psychology professor from Fu Jen Catholic University. On the morning of the 19th, at 8:00 a.m., the second paper reading session was held, including "The English Ability of University Freshmen" by Ai Wei, "A Study on the Methods of Official Examinations" by Shi Meixuan, "Experiments on Two Kinds of Decimal Multiplication and Essay Testing" by Zhou Xuezhang, "Testing Work of the Dingxian Mass Education Promotion Association" by Zhou Xiangeng, "A Comparison of the Writing Speed of Chinese in Horizontal and Vertical Directions" by Cai Lesheng, and "Unrestricted Association of Chinese Children" by Lu Zhiwei. Each of these papers represented years of experiments or the results of numerous studies. It is said that the third issue of the Society's Testing Magazine will publish all of these papers to commemorate the event. In the afternoon of the 19th, an administrative meeting was held to discuss proposals. Important ones included compiling and revising various testing books for primary and secondary schools, popularizing testing knowledge among the masses, and discussing the retention, abolition, or improvement of the TBCF scoring method. It was also suggested that the Ministry of Education should separately establish courses on educational testing and educational statistics for senior high school and normal school education, and suggested that the authorities restore the Department of Education, Department of Psychology, and the merger of the Department of Psychology of Central University with the College of Education. The election of the second Board of Directors resulted in the election of Ai Wei, Chen Heqin, Yi Kejian, Lu Zhiwei, Wang Shulin, Huang Longguang, and Liao Shicheng as directors, and Peng Baichuan, Xiao Xiaorong, and Gu Kebin as alternate directors. On the 20th, all members of the Society visited the Summer Palace and held a picnic, and the meeting was adjourned on the same day.

Local News 91

The Ministry of Education Failed to Take Over Labor University Yesterday

Representatives of Teachers and Students Request Fulfillment of Preconditions

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education specially dispatched three commissioners, Dai Xiashu, Yu Dong, and Sen Wen, to Labor University to negotiate. It happened that the school's school protection committee was holding a meeting, and they immediately elected representatives to inquire with the three commissioners about whether there was a satisfactory solution to the preconditions telegraphed to the Ministry of Education by the Labor University Faculty and Staff School Protection Committee a few days ago: (1) officially announce the Labor University revitalization plan; (2) pay off all arrears in salaries for all faculty and staff. The three commissioners replied that they came to the school "only to handle the takeover, and have not heard about any other issues." The faculty and staff representatives of the school believed that the takeover of Labor University was a whole issue, and they could not only take over without considering the labor costs of the faculty and staff, nor could they come to take over before the Executive Yuan's instruction regarding the temporary nature of the closure of Labor University had been discussed. Therefore, the three commissioners agreed to telegraph the Ministry of Education that day to request on their behalf. Later, student representatives of Labor University also came to inquire with the three commissioners about the arrangements for August's food and lodging expenses and transfer travel expenses. It was not until 12 o'clock that Dai and others agreed to come to the school again the day after tomorrow to answer and fulfill them in person, and then they left the school.

Another News: The faculty and staff of Labor University originally planned to take the night train to Beijing on the 24th of this month to petition, but after hearing that the Ministry of Education had appointed three officials, Dai Xiashu, Yu Dong, and Sen Wen, to Shanghai and would come to the school, they issued an emergency notice to temporarily stop leaving the school. Now they are waiting for the result of the three officials' telegram to the Ministry of Education today before deciding whether to proceed or stop.

Yesterday, the school committee also telegraphed Minister Zhu to inquire why the reorganization plan was not announced if there was one. The original telegram is as follows: "Minister Zhu of the Ministry of Education, Nanjing, in the Shiyeshenbao and Shishi Xinbao, your Excellency announced in the explanation of the government's reorganization of universities that 'the government has carefully decided after a very long discussion on the reorganization plans for Central University, Labor University, Qingdao University, as well as Jinan University, Peiping University, and Normal University,' etc. For Labor University, it has also been carefully discussed for a long time, and there is also a reorganization plan. It should follow the precedent of Central University and Qingdao University and quickly officially announce this reorganization plan to dispel doubts. Respectfully, the Labor University Faculty and Staff School Protection Committee."

Jinan University Alumni Association Telegraphed the Government Yesterday

Requesting the Withdrawal of the Order to Abolish the Colleges of Law and Education

Since the Jinan University Alumni Association was reorganized, its work has been very intense. It is recently heard that the government authorities intend to abolish the Colleges of Law and Education of the alma mater. Feeling that Jinan University has special circumstances, they telegraphed the National Government Central Party Headquarters, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Education, requesting the withdrawal of the order. The telegram is as follows:

(Omitted above) It is our humble opinion that our alma mater, Jinan University, has been established for 26 years. It is not only a higher institution with a long history in the country, but also has the important mission of developing overseas Chinese education. It should be given special care and vigorously promoted. However, your esteemed Yuan and Ministry have decided to abolish the Colleges of Law and Education, which has caused deep suspicion and shock upon hearing the news. The establishment of the College of Education by the alma mater deeply meets the needs of overseas Chinese, and is dedicated to cultivating teachers for overseas Chinese areas. In addition to Soochow University, which was established by the church and is still of a certain scale, the domestic law schools are only in their infancy. The College of Law of the alma mater is to meet the needs of the times, and especially to cultivate diplomatic talents to serve overseas, develop overseas Chinese affairs, and improve the status of overseas Chinese. It should be given special support. Now that the alma mater is improving in time after the war, and is actively reorganizing in recent months, the various facilities for the 21st year have been planned and are in progress, and many teachers and staff have been hired. If your esteemed Yuan and Ministry also cancel the Colleges of Law and Education, the entire school affairs of the alma mater will be extremely difficult. Therefore, we are particularly asking your esteemed Yuan and Ministry to protect the purpose of the overseas Chinese, and quickly withdraw the order to facilitate development. The overseas Chinese are fortunate, and the overseas Chinese education is fortunate. The telegram is urgent.

Davis Cup

US Obtains the Right to Challenge

Europe-America Inter-zonal Final

Germany Fails 2 to 3

Starts This Friday

US and France to Vie for Silver Cup

Paris, 24th (Havas) – In the final day of the Davis Cup Europe-America inter-zonal final between the US and Germany, Vines (US) defeated Krahwinkel (Ger) with scores of 3-6, 6-3, 9-7, and 6-3. At this point, the US had already defeated Germany with a score of 3 to 1. The last match was irrelevant to the outcome but was still played. Von Cramm (Ger) defeated Shields (US) with scores of 6-1, 6-0, 6-8, and 6-2. The overall result was a 3-2 victory for the US, which will compete against France in the challenge round on Friday, Saturday, and Sunday for three days.

Vines Wins Against Krahwinkel Again

Paris, 24th (Havas) – Today was the third day of the Davis Cup match between the US and Germany. The weather was clear and the stands were full. In the first match, Vines (US) played against Krahwinkel (Ger). Both players were extremely popular upon entering the court. In the first set, Krahwinkel’s skills were excellent, winning 6-3. In the first game of the second set, Krahwinkel also won, but Vines unleashed his special skill, using cannonball serves to subdue his opponent. Although Krahwinkel had excellent shots that delighted the spectators, he ultimately could not win. Vines won the second set 6-3. In the third set, both sides seemed tired, and the momentum of the ball was no longer as quick as before. Krahwinkel was sometimes able to put his opponent in a difficult position, but Vines rallied and won the third set 9-7. After a break, the battle resumed, and Vines clearly had the advantage, winning 6-3 and defeating Germany.

Von Cramm Greatly Defeats Shields

Paris, 24th (Havas) – The last match between the US and Germany was Shields (US) against Von Cramm (Ger). Shields' skills were rusty, just like on the first day of the match, while Von Cramm was impeccable. Before long, he was able to control his opponent, winning the first set 6-1. In the second set, Von Cramm won again 6-0. Shields was completely flustered, unable to return even the easiest of shots. However, in the third set, Shields rallied and won 8-6. After a break, the battle resumed, and Von Cramm's skills were still extremely skilled, winning the fourth set 6-2 and defeating Shields. Looking back to when the US and Germany met in 1929, Germany was completely defeated 0-5. Although they failed this time, the score was still 2-3, which is a significant improvement compared to three years ago.

The German Duo Is Truly Formidable

Paris, 24th (Reuters) – In the Davis Cup Europe-America inter-zonal final, the US defeated Germany 3-2 this afternoon, and will compete against France in the challenge final starting on the 29th.

Vines defeated Krahwinkel with scores of 3-6, 6-3, 9-7, and 6-3, deciding the victory. Vines’ victory was entirely due to his powerful smashes, heavy spins, and serves. However, Krahwinkel's positioning, placement, and returns were all magnificent and steady. Krahwinkel only double-faulted twice in the entire match, while Vines double-faulted as many as nine times.

Von Cramm defeated Shields 6-1, 6-0, 6-8, 6-2. The match was unusually dull, and the disparity in skill was too great.

France Announces Full Team Lineup

Paris, 24th (Havas) – After the match between the US and Germany, the Technical Committee of the French Tennis Association met to finalize the French team participating in the Davis Cup. The committee then issued the following announcement: "The chairman of this committee, in light of Lacoste's sudden illness and inability to represent France in the Davis Cup challenge round, feels compelled to rely on Borotra. He has earnestly persuaded Borotra to sacrifice his spirit and remain loyal to the French tennis team by rescinding his decision to no longer play singles matches. Borotra, who always loves discipline, has fully and unreservedly agreed to this request, stating that the committee should appoint a young player if possible. As such, this association has finalized the organization of the French team, which includes Borotra, Brugnon, Boussus, and Cochet. The captain is Gillou."

Enthusiastic Participants in Summer Football

Registration Will Close at the End of the Month

At this time of oppressive heat, the football sport, which is most popular and well-loved by Shanghai residents, is quiet and unknown, and there is a saying that it is not suitable for the season. However, if we continue to adhere to the established rules, it would be like abandoning food because of choking, making it impossible for football skills to advance. The National Sports Advancement Association, in view of this, has created the innovation of shortening the game time for both the summer and inter-business competitions, with good intentions. In addition, the enthusiastic Mr. Dong Zhenyuan and the Taiping Company have produced and donated two large silver cups as trophies for the two competitions to encourage participation. Since registration began on the 18th of this month, the Qinghua, Xingguang, Yuqing (changed from Xuhui), Lingnan, Huadong Company, Zhihua, Yuequn, and Qiangnan teams have participated in the summer league, and the Taiping Insurance Company, Zhonghua Bookstore, Postal Team, and Land Bureau teams have participated in the inter-business cup. However, there are many football teams in Shanghai, and there are certainly many companies and firms that have entire teams. At that time, during leisure time after work, as the setting sun falls (games start after 5 PM), practicing skills on the green is truly unparalleled entertainment for physical fitness. Registration for the competition will close on the 31st of this month, so it is best to register as soon as possible.

Business News

Finance 93

Gold Price Drops 4.6 Taels

Swap Market Advance Bids at 1.9 Taels Yesterday, the gold price indeed continued to fall, with relatively smooth fluctuations. Throughout the day, the high and low prices varied by about five taels, eventually falling more than four taels. The buying and selling activities of various parties were uneven, and the sentiment among dealers was weak. Initially, the silver market reported a slight decrease due to price increases, but it became weaker due to large-scale selling. Although the foreign exchange market extended half a notch, the domestic market went from loose to flat. Buyers in the market were also active, and short sellers took advantage of this to advance, causing the price to rise by three or four taels. The market then dipped again, but the overall situation was mediocre, with the final price recorded at about 743 taels. The price for August delivery was once swapped at 1.9 taels, still with advance bids from the long side. The detailed conditions of the market before and after are recorded below.

Large Sellers Cause Gold Prices to Fall Further From the Early Opening of September

Delivery at 747.5 taels, slightly lower by 0.4 taels. Although the British and American silver markets each rose by one-eighth yesterday, it did not have a significant impact. Subsequently, Dahsingyong, Yuanheng, Hengyu, Yifungyong, Hengxing, Dadecheng, Xinchang, and Yuankangxiang successively sold aggressively. It was rumored that Mr. Wu Heng had to unload, and because the US dollar was becoming weaker, the July price was initially at 81.25, which HSBC and Banque de l'Indochine then sold to Zhejiang for 30 yuan. In addition, Mercury offered September British gold at 18.25, so the gold price continued to fall. Nearing 9:30, it suddenly dropped to 41.8 taels, but Tongtaichang quickly covered their short positions and then picked up 1.0 taels to 43 taels. British gold opened with a high bid of 1.125, and the US dollar was the same. When it retreated to 42.2 taels, news suddenly came that Citibank was buying, with July US dollars at 93.75. Banque de l'Indochine also bought, and because Tongtaichang's buying momentum was strong, Hengyu, Yifungyong, and Yuanxingyong and Fuyu reversed and bought in, adding another 2 taels to the price, reaching 45 taels at around 10:20. However, there was fluctuation within a few cents in half an hour. Later, Zhifengyong, Dadecheng, Fuyu, and Zhaofengchang sold, so August British gold was paired at 0.25, down more than 1 tael. At 11:00, it was 43.3 taels, and it immediately turned upward, because Mercury was absorbing July US dollars at 93.75, and October was paired at 30.01875 yuan. There were also many buyers on the floor. Hengxing, Tongtaichang, Hongkangyong, Yuantai, Zhaofengchang, Chengdayong, Yuanmaoyong and others were all buying in. Yarn Flowers 95

Recently, yarn prices have surged by two or three taels.

Yarn sales are booming... Chinese factories' remaining stock has been completely bought up.

The actual demand for cotton yarn is increasingly developing. Merchants from Hunan and Guangdong continue to purchase incessantly, and current yarn supplies have been bought out. They are now purchasing futures with delivery dates of eight, nine, or thirteen months, with increasingly larger quantities. People's sentiment is extremely excited, and the market is steadily rising. The reason for this is that this year, the Yangtze River basin has had consistent rainfall, resulting in a bountiful harvest. Therefore, many operators are preparing for potential future needs by purchasing in large quantities, creating a sudden and vibrant market. This month, only one factory is delivering contract yarn, and all the chips have been taken by buyers. General short sellers, seeing the good spot sales, are even more panicked. The market has surged by three taels and three qian. However, the global cotton industry is still sluggish, while domestic demand in the South is booming. This time, Chinese factories' remaining stock has been completely sold out, which is a good sign for our country's textile industry.

Contract prices rise, especially for this month's futures. The contract market opened with robust spot yarn trading. Merchants from the Yangtze River region also began purchasing, boosting confidence. There was a lack of sellers in the market, and short sellers covered their positions. This month's futures rose by two taels, while distant futures rose by five or six qian. Customers continued to purchase actively in the second and third sessions, tightening the market further, and prices rose another three or six qian. In the end, prices for all months rose by one to three taels and three qian. In the afternoon, the market remained closed due to the heat. A total of 40,150 bales of contract yarn were traded.
