Letter from the Save-by-Cutting-Down-and-Eating-Less Society to Members in Other Cities 126

Reporting on the Initiation Process

Organizing Branches in Other Cities

The Chinese National Save-by-Cutting-Down-and-Eating-Less Society sent a letter to its members in other cities yesterday, stating: "In response to your previous letter, we learned that you share our sympathy for the society's purpose and intend to join. Because the society is in the process of applying to the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters for permission to organize, we did not dare to reply rashly to letters from comrades in other cities before obtaining the Party Headquarters' permission, causing you to be anxious. We apologize for this. The society was initially founded by a small number of comrades and named the 'Save-on-Clothing-and-Food Comrades Society.' There was no consideration at the time. Later, more and more comrades joined in this city, and the National Government issued a nationwide decree on May 11, instructing the people to practice cutting down on clothing and food, and to strive for production to save the country. Therefore, some comrades in the society proposed to change the name to the 'Chinese National Save-by-Cutting-Down-and-Eating-Less Society' in accordance with the spirit of the National Government's instructions, in order to expand publicity and establish branches in various places, and to formulate the general rules of the General Assembly and the organizational procedures of the branches. The third meeting of the initiators passed the proposal and submitted it to the Party Headquarters for record. Now, we have obtained the permission of the Party Headquarters and established a preparatory committee on the 17th of this month. The following eleven standing committee members were elected: Wu Banping, Chen Guangxiang, Sun Bin, Li Junpan, Pan Tianyi, Sha Shouzhong, Shen Yunyu, Li Zhineng, Wu Biaomin, Liang Gengshun, and Ren Nongxuan, and they were assigned to the five sections of 'Solicitation,' 'Publicity,' 'Investigation,' 'Documentation,' and 'Accounting' to be responsible for the preparation. This is the entire process of the society from its inception to the present. We are very grateful for the concern of the comrades for the society. We are sending you a copy of the society's constitution and a copy of the organizational procedures of the branch for your inspection. If you can invite comrades to organize branches in your area and jointly promote progress, we would be extremely fortunate."

The Emei Steamer Grounded and Damaged 127

China Merchants Bureau's Emei steamer, sailing from Shanghai to Chongqing, loaded cargo downstream in Chongqing on the morning of the 21st of this month. At noon, when it arrived at the Yanzhuba area, the ship was grounded in a shoal due to the rushing water. After repeated efforts by the shipowner, Mr. Ji, the Emei was pulled out during high tide half an hour later and returned to Yichang. A telegram reported yesterday morning that the Emei steamer floated up at the grounding site and sailed to Yichang without any initial damage. However, when the cargo was unloaded on the 24th, it was discovered that the keel, iron pillars, and platforms of the second cabin were all bent and damaged due to the grounding. The shipping department has reported to the General Manager Li to review the repair plan for the ship.

Taihu Bandit Chief 128

Wang Yucheng and Nine Others Arrested

Taihu bandit chief Wang Yucheng, also known as Shi Changqing, gathered his followers and specialized in looting at the junction of Jiangsu and Songjiang, such as robbing the Lakezhou steamer, robbing over forty boxes of cigarettes from the Nanyang Tobacco Company, over a hundred bundles of cotton yarn from Tao Jianji Yarn Company, and countless other robberies. Later, the Jiangsu-Songjiang Bandit Suppression Headquarters dispatched troops to suppress them severely, but Wang escaped the law. Therefore, the headquarters specifically ordered Detective Captain Xu Fengshan to arrest him. After receiving the order, Captain Xu came to Shanghai to investigate. He found that the bandit was hiding on a yellow sand ship No. 6012 at Guangxing Wharf in front of the Renchang Soap Factory in Yangshupu, and all the people on the ship were bandits, with two pistols and one Mauser pistol. Captain Xu then reported to the Water Patrol Police Station. The Western Detective Belikas, Chinese Detectives Sun Ajia and Hu Changqing, etc., along with Captain Xu, rushed to the scene and arrested Wang Yucheng, Zhou Menglin, Cui Desheng, Yang Zhengqing, Sun Youzhong, Wu Zhusan, Zhou Bailin, Tang Mingzhou, Tang Youlin, and nine others. During the arrest, the criminals hid their weapons in bags and threw them into the river in an attempt to destroy the evidence. However, Captain Xu showed the arrest warrant and took them all to the police station and sent them to the local court. Captain Xu requested the transfer. The prosecutor ordered them to prepare documents and come to the case to welcome the investigation.

Tragedy Occurs While Collecting Scrap Copper 129

An Explosion Injures Four People

Jin Jincheng, a 45-year-old from Shaoxing, opened the Huidacontin Copper and Tin Store at No. 8, Minguo Lane, Minguo Road, in the French Concession, buying all kinds of scrap copper and old tin for profit. During the Shanghai battle this year, many abandoned guns, cannons, shells and copper casings were left in the northern part of Shanghai, and laborers competed to pick them up and sell them to copper and tin shops, so many of them relied on this to make a profit. Jin opened a copper shop and could not be an exception. However, at 11:35 yesterday morning, Jin personally supervised his partners Ding Yifang (22 years old), Jin Guangshun (21 years old), and apprentice Chen Xiadong (15 years old) in front of the hall of the shop to identify and sort out two large sacks of copper casings. Unexpectedly, there was a live bullet mixed in. Jin did not pay attention and hit it hard with an iron hammer. Suddenly, the explosives detonated with a loud bang, shaking the neighborhood. Apprentice Chen Xiadong was more seriously injured and was immediately taken to the hospital for treatment. The other three were slightly injured and were also sent to the hospital for diagnosis and treatment. The French Concession police heard the news and are now sending detectives to investigate thoroughly. They must actively ban such illegal purchases of shell copper shops.

Farmers Hope for Rain 130

Recently, the weather in this city has been unusually hot, with the Fahrenheit thermometer reaching around 100 degrees, causing epidemics to rage everywhere and the rural farmland to be extremely dry. According to farmers in the western suburbs of Shanghai and Pudong, it has not rained for almost a month, and the farmland is dry and cracked. Farmers are pumping water day and night, and they are exhausted and anxious. Moreover, due to the drying up of rivers and the scorching sun, pumping water day and night is useless, so the rice has been affected. If it does not rain soon, there will be a drought.

First Special Court Incinerates Poisons 131

The Shanghai First Special District Court, in accordance with regulations, publicly incinerates confiscated prohibited items such as opium and raw opium every three months to emphasize the prohibition of smoking. While the public sale of opium is being touted, the court is still very strict in handling opium cases. Now that the time for incineration has arrived again, President Zhou designated the Yizhongdi of the Baoantang Hall on the south side of the North Zhejiang Road Court as the incineration site. At 8:00 yesterday morning, court clerks moved the opium, opium paste, red pills, and smoking paraphernalia confiscated in the last three months from the confiscated property warehouse to the site and burned them with dry firewood and kerosene. Court police were dispatched to the scene to supervise. In addition, several prosecutors from the court and the Second Branch of the High Court came to the scene to supervise. The Municipal Council also sent representatives to visit. The incineration was completed at around 2:00 in the afternoon.

Private Counterfeit Coin Factory Cracked in Tongzhou Road 132

Yang Deji, a native of Shaoxing, colluded with Wang Daosheng, a native of Jiangbei, to privately manufacture counterfeit coins at No. 124 Tongzhou Road, and sold them in the market to make profits. Many people were harmed by it. Sun Zhenqing, a Chinese detective from the Jiaxing Road Police Station, found out about the matter. Together with Western detectives, they went secretly at 2:00 AM yesterday morning and arrested Yang and Wang at the address. They confiscated 37 counterfeit coins, two models, an iron stove, etc. They also searched Wang's home at No. 76 Ruijin Road and found batteries, medicine powder, and rubber stamps. They took them all to the police station and then sent them to the First Special District Court. The police lawyer, Chen Ming, presented the case and submitted the confiscated counterfeit coins for inspection. When questioned, the defendant Yang Deji confessed that he had lost his job recently. Wang Daosheng had asked him to go to No. 124 Tongzhou Road to continue this business for the late Jin Alin, but he had not yet taken over when he was arrested by the police. Wang Daosheng confessed that these models and other items were all left behind by the late Jin Alin. Jin died on June 25. Yang Deji was indeed asked by him to do it, but only for one day. Jin Alin had been in this counterfeit coin business for two years and could buy 16 or 17 coins for each foreign coin. Judge Shen reviewed the confession and ordered them to be remanded in custody and sentenced on a fixed date.

Autopsy on Russian Woman Who Committed Suicide by Shooting 133

At around 6:00 AM the day before yesterday, a Russian woman named Masli Kofur, 30 years old, residing at No. 14 Suzhou Road, suddenly went to Room 602 on the sixth floor of HSBC Housing at No. 56 Sichuan Road, the residence of Westerner Kaing Tai, Deputy Chief Patrol of the Central Police Station. She appeared to be drunk. The Westerner had not yet gotten out of bed and asked her what she was doing there. The Russian woman replied that she was very sorry. Kaing Tai drove her out of the room. Unexpectedly, the woman broke into the next room (which was also rented by Kai) and took out a pistol used by Kai from the closet and fired three shots at her head and chest, falling to the ground immediately and bleeding profusely. Then Miao Huating, the Chinese clerk hired by Kai, heard the noise and went in to inspect, seeing her lying in a pool of blood. He immediately ran to inform his master and reported to the Central Police Station, which dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. They sent her to the Public Concession Hospital for treatment, but she died. The body was taken to the Ferren Road Mortuary. Yesterday morning, Zhan Liangce, prosecutor of the First Special District Court, was commissioned to come to the mortuary to examine the body and sit in court. According to Kaing Tai's (transliteration) statement, the deceased was a friend of his and there was no relationship of any kind. He was still sleeping that day when she suddenly broke into his bedroom. Seeing that she appeared to be drunk, he drove her out. Unexpectedly, she went to his next room to commit suicide. According to Miao Huating's statement of the situation at the time, Mr. Zhan ordered the examination to confirm that the deceased Russian woman, Masli Kofur, had indeed died by shooting herself with a pistol. The body was handed over to her aunt, Siber Nara, who signed an undertaking to take it back for coffin burial.

False Mortgage List for Borrowing Money 134

Zhengda Bank Files a Lawsuit

Huang Zhiqing and Zou Jiabai Accused

Huang Zhiqing, manager of Lianchang Company, previously fabricated a list of all the properties of Chongming Electric Power Co., Ltd. in Chongming County due to the company's financial exhaustion. Together with Zou Jiabai, he mortgaged it to Zhengda Bank for a loan of 30,000 taels of silver, with the redemption period set for January 19th of the 20th year. However, after the deadline, neither the principal nor the interest was repaid. The bank then sued the Chongming County Government. When Shi Yuming and other shareholders of the Chongming Electric Light Company learned of this, they also filed a statement, stating that Huang Zhiqing's claim that the electric light factory was purchased by him was false. Huang had absolutely no mortgage right. Later, during the trial in Chongming County, Huang also admitted that the mortgage list was fabricated. In May of this year, the Chongming County Government had already ruled that the mortgage contract signed by Zhengda Bank and the two defendants, Huang and Zou, was invalid. After receiving the verdict, Zhengda negotiated with Huang and others to recover the money, but to no avail. Now, based on the verdict of the Chongming County Government, the bank has filed a criminal self-accusation against Huang and Zou with the First Special District Court for forging documents and fraudulently obtaining money. It is said that the court will open a trial soon.

Opium and Cars Confiscated 135

Hong Maoting and Others Sentenced for Smuggling Opium

Hong Maoting, a native of Yangzhou, residing at No. 6, Bu Lin Lane, Zhengjia Muqiao Street, in the French Concession, hired Zhu Yibiao, a car driver from the Shijie Car Company on Edward Road, driving car number 11689, to transport opium at the Taikoo Wharf at 4:45 AM on the 10th of this month. Ge Xilai (transliteration), a head constable from the Xiaodongmen French Concession Police Station, discovered this while patrolling. During the inspection, Xu Xiangkun handed the constable a roll of banknotes, worth several hundred yuan, and asked him to refrain from investigating. As the constable was about to arrest them, Hong and Zhu drove away, only Xu was caught. Subsequently, Western detectives Mu Bikun Chonggen, Mao Jinsheng, Deputy Detectives Wang Rusong, Jiang Changwen, and detectives Bao Tan Gu Hongzhou and Lu Jinxiang were dispatched to investigate. Forty-eight pounds of opium were seized in the compartment of the chartered car in the hall of No. 6 Bu Lin Lane, and Hong was arrested. Car driver Zhu Yibiao and the car were also arrested and sent to the Second Special Court. They were prosecuted in accordance with Article 6 of the Anti-Smoking Law. After Judge Wang Gangxu of the Criminal Court tried the case, he announced the end of the debate. Yesterday was the sentencing date. At 9:30 AM, Judge Wang took his seat in Criminal Court One and ordered the defendants to be brought to the court. Hong Maoting was sentenced to ten months of imprisonment and fined 1,200 yuan for the crime of possessing opium with the intent to sell it. Zhu Yibiao was sentenced to eight months of imprisonment and fined 1,000 yuan for the crime of helping to transport opium with the intent to sell it. Xu Xiangkun was sentenced to eight months of imprisonment and fined 1,000 yuan for the crime of helping to transport opium with the intent to sell it, and sentenced to four months of imprisonment and fined 200 yuan for the crime of bribing public officials in connection with their duties, with a total imprisonment of nine months and a fine of 1,100 yuan. If the fines are converted into imprisonment, three yuan shall be calculated as one day, and the time limit shall not exceed one year. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized shall be offset by two days for one day of imprisonment. Forty-eight pounds of opium and car number 11689 shall be confiscated.

China Merchants Public Bus Company 136

Requesting Exemption from Autumn Vehicle Tax

Municipal Government Directives Approved

The China Merchants Public Bus Company of this city, whose business scope is entirely in the Zhabei area, has been struggling to maintain transportation since the retreat of Japanese soldiers. It first restored the No. 3 route (North Station to Zhenru), while the No. 1 route (North Station to Jiangwan) has not yet been opened due to the fact that the Japanese soldiers stationed in Area D of 63 Huahui have just withdrawn and the Yokohama Bridge has not yet been repaired. All expenses rely solely on the income from the No. 3 route. However, due to the desolation after the war, the income from this route is also very meager, making it difficult to support the company. Therefore, it submitted a document to the Municipal Public Works Bureau a few days ago, requesting that the autumn vehicle tax be waived entirely to reduce expenses and alleviate the business's difficulties. Director Huang of the Municipal Public Works Bureau, believing that the company's statement was true, forwarded the request to the municipal government for instructions. Yesterday, the municipal government held a directive to the Public Works Bureau, stating, "Noted. Since the China Merchants Public Bus Company claims that the business of Route 3 is meager and it is difficult to support it, which is true, it should be allowed to specifically exempt the vehicle tax for Route 3 for the autumn season of this year to show consideration. In addition to informing the Finance Bureau, you should also inform them."

Suicide by Poisoning After Unsuccessful Job Search 137

Ye Bingchu's Situation is Pitiful

Ye Bingchu, a 37-year-old from Ningbo, who usually resides in his hometown, came to Shanghai on the 18th of this month and booked Room 16 at the Huibin Hotel on Shandong Road. On the 22nd, he suddenly secretly bought opium and committed suicide. Later, a tea waiter named Chen Jingxiong heard shouting outside his door, realized that something was wrong, and pushed the door open. He saw that Ye's face had changed drastically, white foam was coming from his mouth, and he was sleeping on the bed. The tea waiter immediately reported to the accounting room, which reported to the Laozha Police Station. Detectives were ordered to investigate and sent him to Renji Hospital for treatment, but he died of poisoning at 5:20 yesterday morning. The body was taken to the Ferren Road Mortuary. At around 10:00, Zhan Liangce, prosecutor of the First Special District Court, was commissioned to come to the mortuary to examine the body and sit in court. According to Wang Bingzhong's statement, he resides at No. 17 Jinhua Street and runs a cigarette shop. The deceased was his cousin. He did not know about it at the time. Later, someone told him that he had poisoned himself. His wife died of illness last year, and his son died this spring. He came to Shanghai to look for a job, but there was no suitable occupation. He met with him a few days ago, and during the conversation, he heard him express resentment. Unexpectedly, he would poison himself. After receiving the statement, Mr. Zhan ordered the examination to confirm that the deceased, Ye Bingchu, had indeed died from opium poisoning. The body was handed over to his cousin, Wang Bingzhong, who signed an undertaking to take it back for coffin burial.

Lianyu Highway 139

Committee for Fundraising Public Bonds in Shanghai Established

The Anhui Lianyu Highway (from Lian County to Yulingguan) has been decided by the Anhui Provincial Government to issue 500,000 yuan of Lianyu Road public bonds, and the Construction Department has sent letters to Xu Jiashi and other Anhui natives in Shanghai to serve as members of the public bond fundraising committee. It is reported that 200,000 yuan of these public bonds have been subscribed by fellow villagers in Shanghai, 100,000 yuan by fellow villagers in Hangzhou, and the remaining 200,000 yuan by fellow villagers in the six counties of Anhui and other ports. It is reported that the Public Bond Fundraising Committee Office in Shanghai has been set up at No. 21 Hongxiang Lane, Xinzha Road, and has been formally established to start work. The office hours are scheduled from 2:00 PM to 5:00 PM every day.

Letters 144

To the Editor, I am writing to you because I read in the "Local News" section of your newspaper on the 25th regarding two articles, "Commander Resigns and Remains," and "Military Law Review to Hear a Large Number of Communists on a Regular Basis," which were said to be statements issued by Chen Hanzu of the Military Law Review. After investigation, I have not met with any correspondents or reporters recently, nor have I made any such statements. Moreover, since the martial law in Shanghai, the Military Law Review has sent all undecided cases to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters for handling in accordance with Article 7 of the Emergency Punishment Law. It has not yet resumed operations. The case of hearing a large number of communists on a regular basis is even more inconsistent with the facts. I hereby request a correction. Respectfully yours, Chen Hanzu, July 25.

To the Editor, I am writing to you regarding the news "The Municipal Government Passes the Reduction and Exemption of Field Taxes in the War Zone" published in the "Local News" section of your newspaper on July 24. The third item of the consultation results of the three bureaus of land, finance, and society, "The remaining districts, except for the two districts of South Shanghai and Pusong, plan to generally reduce the busy season tax by 20%," should be ""The two districts of South Shanghai and Pusong plan to generally reduce the busy season tax by 20%." Please correct it accordingly. Sincerely, Propaganda Section of the Second Department of the Shanghai Municipal Government, July 25.

To the Editor, I am writing to you because I read in today's newspaper a local news article about the establishment of a temporary post office by the Shanghai-Japan Consulate after the postal blockade in the Northeast. I was very surprised to read it. After investigation, this record is completely untrue and may easily cause misunderstandings among Chinese and foreigners. Together, I urgently send a letter to ensure that your newspaper quickly corrects it and publishes this letter so that it can be widely known and show the facts. This is where I feel grateful. Sincerely, Consulate General of Japan in Shanghai, July 25. To the Editor, I am writing to you regarding the article "Division Commander Fan Shisheng Injured and Comes to Shanghai" published in your newspaper recently. After investigation, the reporter of the Guowen News Agency mistakenly took our Division Commander "Shaozeng" and Division Commander Fan "Shisheng" as one person. In fact, our Division Commander's name commonly used is "Shaozeng," and Division Commander Fan Shisheng is still alive and well in central Hubei at this moment. In addition, the biggest reason for our Division Commander's change of location for medical treatment this time is still the climate. Together, I make a statement for correction. Sincerely, Fan Zhongqu, July 25.

Free Talk

Summer Riddles (Part 1) 146

— Zhan Lu

Tan Zhi One Two

Under the shade of the green pagoda trees, a temporary club is organized: a rattan chair every five steps, a bamboo couch every ten steps. While family members chat idly, they inevitably guess a few riddles to help pass the summer heat.

Gentlemen, using this small garden surrounded by bamboo fences in "Free Talk" as our place to cool off after work; guessing riddles is indispensable for passing the time while relaxing. One | Two | Three | My riddles, like commands, consist of three in total.

First, who is it that sings the tune of a tyrannical emperor when the scorching sun is overhead?

|| This tyrannical emperor is not a real emperor. It would be wrong to guess Puyi.

Second, if a certain idiom from the Zuo Zhuan were effective, then Chongguang's precious leg would never have been cut off. Now that Chongguang has become a one-legged Kui, it is clear that a certain idiom from the Zuo Zhuan is unreliable. What is this idiom called? || The idiom from Zuo Zhuan guarantees that Chongguang's leg would not be cut off. Those who have read Zuo Zhuan should be able to guess it easily.

Third, there is a five-character couplet that looks the same whether read forward or backward, called || Support Ma Yuan Support Ma Yuan. To match it with a lower line of the same nature, and also relevant to the current situation, what is this lower line called? || The "yuan" in "support Ma" accepts both level and oblique tones; now it is specified to be used as an oblique tone. Ma Yuan was a famous general, used as a metaphor for General Ma Zhanshan. You must also find an ancient person for these five characters, and also use them as a metaphor for a modern person. This kind of antithesis is unique and resembles guessing riddles.

Gentlemen cooling off, goodbye for now; after asking for a day, I will reveal the answers to you in this small garden.

A Eulogy for Ye Huijun 147

— Hu Wanxuan

Mr. Ye Huijun, a prominent figure in the business world, was loyal, courageous, and upright. He made great contributions to the recovery of Shanghai during the Xinhai Revolution. Without the strength of the merchant corps at that time, the capture of Shanghai could not have been achieved so quickly. Otherwise, Nanjing could not have been captured quickly, and the Qing court's reinforcements would have driven down from Jiangpu, making the situation critical and hopeless. A single mistake could have ruined everything. Mr. Ye truly contributed to the Republic of China.

Later, when Xiangcheng (Yuan Shikai) declared himself emperor, he feared that Mr. Ye would be a thorn in his side and offered a reward for his capture. Therefore, Mr. Ye fled to Japan, enduring hardship. After returning to China, he did not consider himself one of the revolutionary pioneers because of this. He devoted himself to business and had no intention of pursuing an official career. However, wherever justice lay, he rushed to it eagerly. He never shirked from local public welfare, no matter how much toil or complaint it entailed. Although he was already over seventy years old, he still served society tirelessly. Now, the sad news has arrived that Mr. Ye suddenly passed away from an abdominal tumor. His legacy is admired, but our thoughts are in vain. It truly makes one feel unbearable sorrow.

Mr. Ye had a sincere nature and treated people and handled affairs with utmost sincerity. However, he held strict views and would directly criticize others' wrongdoings, even in crowded places. Honest words are harsh to the ear, and some people resented him for this. However, on the day after Mr. Ye's death, many of those who had held grudges against him came to pay their respects. Some even wept loudly, showing how deeply Mr. Ye moved people.

Mr. Ye was born posthumously and came from a poor family with no means for schooling. At the age of fourteen, he came to Shanghai to learn the rice business. He was respectful, diligent, and devoted to his work. In his spare time, he studied diligently. Even at his advanced age, he still practiced calligraphy and read every morning without fail. Regarding his integrity and honesty, never taking even the smallest thing improperly, the people of Shanghai all know this. It is remembered that a certain influential figure sent someone with generous gifts. Mr. Ye firmly refused to accept them, and the servant insisted that Mr. Ye accept them, even arguing back. Mr. Ye then angrily tied him outside the door. Those who heard of this all praised it as a fine story.

It is said that Mr. Ye's abdominal tumor lasted for three months. Before that, the government convened a National Crisis Conference in Luoyang, and Mr. Ye was also invited to be a member. At that time, he had been ill for many days. His family tried to dissuade him, but he would not listen. After struggling to go to the capital, he collapsed in an inn. So he returned to Shanghai, but his illness had already become terminal. He went to Guangci

Hospital for treatment. The French director, who was skilled in medicine, said that there was a newly invented radium therapy that could cure Mr. Ye's illness, but the fee was as high as two thousand gold coins. Mr. Ye had no way to pay it, and he was unwilling to receive treatment because the consultation fee was so high. His sons ran around in many ways, but they were unable to raise the full amount in time. Furthermore, Mr. Ye insisted on leaving the hospital, so he returned without receiving treatment. Later, he was diagnosed and treated by Chinese and foreign doctors, but he was ultimately unable to recover.

When Mr. Ye was bedridden, he was sometimes delirious, and what he said was mostly about public welfare. One day, Mr. Wang Xiaolai went to visit him. Mr. Ye was in a state of semi-consciousness. Suddenly, he started talking about the city's municipal problems, speaking eloquently. Mr. Wang just responded with "yes, yes."

In summary, Mr. Ye devoted his life to the local area. Last year, he purchased several houses in Shanghai, which had almost exhausted his savings from seventy years of diligence and thrift. The construction cost was still several thousand yuan short, which his sons managed to raise to pay off. He had hoped to enjoy a peaceful old age in his later years, but heaven did not grant him that. The country and society have lost a pillar, and we mourn him endlessly.

Island Musings 148

— Huang Ren

Forget Your Toothache Toothaches are a disease that everyone fears. Once it starts to hurt, it's worse than being executed. Although there are dentists to consult, the difficulties of extracting or filling teeth also make people tremble with fear. That

Twenty minutes on the reclining chair is like a death row inmate sitting in an electric chair. But now, a British dentist has come up with a great idea to make you forget your toothache. He has you sit in his reclining chair, and immediately a small screen is placed where your eyes can see it. Then, Charlie Chaplin, Rock, and Pescator appear on the screen one by one, making all kinds of ridiculous and funny movements, causing you to laugh involuntarily from the bottom of your heart. For a moment, you forget about your toothache. He takes this opportunity to put the little gadget in your mouth and forcefully pulls out your bad tooth. You don't even feel it at all. Isn't this method good news for toothache comrades?

Speed-loving Women In mid-June of this year, two British female race car experts will compete with several male race car experts in a 1,000-mile race at Brooklands to determine who is the best. This is a recent shocking event in the sports world. From our observation, modern women generally love speed. Three years ago, a noblewoman, Mrs. V. Bruce, ran 2,150 miles in 24 hours, averaging 89.57 miles per hour, breaking the world record. She got tired of playing with race cars and started playing with airplanes. She made several long-distance flights and even circumnavigated the world by plane and mail ship. She truly deserves to be called a heroine.

Mrs. M.T. Hickey, America's most famous speedboat expert, was a sickly person three years ago. The most painful thing was neurasthenia, which even doctors couldn't cure. One day, she sat on the riverbank watching men compete in speedboat races and became very excited. She asked her husband to buy her a speedboat. The first time she got on the boat, she was so weak that she needed help getting on. But now, she is a famous speedboat racer in the New World.

Rat Thief 149

— Tan Zhuoming

The world is deteriorating, and people's hearts are not as good as before. Cases of theft are heard every day, and the techniques are becoming increasingly strange. Exhausting all possibilities, I heard a friend talk about a rat thief case yesterday. The thief was able to use chemistry to commit theft. This is a novel incident and worth recording.

In a certain town in Zhongshan County, Guangdong, there was a pawnshop with considerable capital and good business. Last month, it suddenly reported a theft. The pawnshop had strict defenses, so it was suspected that it was not an outside thief. A certain partner, Mr. Jia, was in charge of guarding the warehouse and had an opium addiction. Everyone suspected him, but they couldn't dismiss him without cause. While investigating, another theft occurred.

The pawnshop had a secret ditch that led to a secluded street behind it. One day, the owner of the pawnshop passed by the area and suddenly saw a huge rat carrying a bag, wriggling out of the ditch. He found it strange and caught it. He opened the bag, and it was full of items from the pawnshop. While he was wondering, Mr. Jia suddenly tiptoed over. The pawnshop owner understood and confronted him. The case was revealed.

Initially, Mr. Jia kept a rat and was very fond of it. When he was smoking opium, he jokingly gave it water that had been used to wipe his smoking utensils. Over time, it became addicted and had to drink it every day, just like a person with an addiction. Mr. Jia's opium addiction was very deep, and his income was not enough to cover his expenses. So he took a risk and thought about stealing from the pawnshop. However, according to the rules of the pawnshop in that area, those guarding the warehouse had to be inspected by the pawnshop owner when entering and exiting, so there was no way to carry anything out. He happened to see the rat's opium addiction acting up and came up with this plan. First, he brought the rat to the pawnshop and released it into the ditch, and placed water mixed with opium at the exit of the ditch behind the pawnshop. He led it to drink. Then, he tied the stolen goods to its back. When the rat's addiction acted up, it would carry the bag out to drink, and the theft was accomplished.

Brief News Since its publication, the Coral Bi-Monthly has been praised by readers. Therefore, pre-orders have come from as far away as America and the Philippines. The second issue has been published on schedule and will no longer be sold individually. Pre-orders in July are only three yuan. The prizes for the fourth issue can be revealed. At the same time, there is a second solicitation, which makes it very interesting.

Worth Recommending National Product Factories (10) 150

— He Gongxing

Soda is an essential item for washing away oil stains. The native soda that China used in the past was produced in Shandong and other places. Since the import of foreign soda, native soda has gradually been abandoned by the Chinese. Later, more and more soda factories were established by Chinese in Shanghai. As a result, foreigners only import soda ash for making soda, and block soda is no longer imported. To date, there are eight soda factories in Shanghai. The larger ones include Henry on Xiaojiu Hua Street, Lida on Zhangjiabang in Pudong, Yongmaoxiang on Limapu Road in Nanshi, and Taikang on Tangshan Road.

Soda is bought by the square, each square weighing about 130 catties. The market price is over five foreign yuan. The total annual sales in Shanghai are worth about 400,000 foreign yuan.

Soda ash is mostly sold by the British company Bunneman in Shanghai. Those made by Chinese themselves include Yongli Company in Tianjin, which is currently managed by Jiuda Refined Salt Company on Baike Road in Shanghai. The market price is about seven taels and several qian of silver per dan, and the price of foreign goods is similar. According to people in the industry, domestic goods are actually better than foreign goods when compared. The reason is that soda ash is like cement. If it is exposed to wind and moisture, it will lose its effectiveness. Bunneman powder is shipped from abroad, and careless handling can often reduce its leavening power. Domestic goods are easier to obtain, so there is no need to worry about exposure to moisture. Its manufacturing

Its manufacturing is done by hand. For every 100 catties of soda ash, 30 catties of cleansing powder (i.e., baking soda) are mixed in with water. After mixing, it is poured into a square frame made of giant tinplate. The frame must be detachable, otherwise, it will not be easy to remove it after it solidifies. The market price of cleansing powder is about eleven taels of silver per dan, excluding foreign goods.

(10) (8) Candle Factory

The raw material for candles is only paraffin (i.e., extracted from kerosene). It is melted in a pot to a certain degree and poured into tinplate molds. Candle wicks are pre-placed in the molds. After it solidifies, it becomes a candle. Large-sized ones can produce 80 candles at a time, while small-sized ones can only produce 40. Shanghai has three factories that manufacture candle wicks: Sanyou and Samsung are the most famous. Each package of 2,000 feet costs about one foreign yuan. As for paraffin, it is exclusively managed by the foreign company Asia Petroleum Company. The market price is over 20 foreign yuan per dan.

Candles are wholesaled by the box, with six candles per tube. The weight varies, but 12 taels is common. Each box contains 25 tubes. The market price per box for those weighing 12 taels is about four foreign yuan. The larger candle factories in Shanghai include Henry on Xiaojiu Hua Street, Nanyang on Lapa Bridge, and Huali on Laiyi Wharf. Last year, their sales of candles each totaled around 70,000 to 80,000 boxes. Others, such as Nanxie Xing and Hengxingyu on Limapu Road, Liantai Xin (i.e., Wuzhou Candle Factory) on Xinzha Road, Lida in Pudong, Qinchang in Hongkou, and Yuqingfeng in Dongjiadu, are also well-known. In total, there are nine candle factories in Shanghai. However, the sales of British Baileishi candles in China increase year by year, with annual sales of three to four million yuan, which is quite alarming.

Striking the Bell at the Ancient Temple (55) 151

— Bu Chu Ting Cao Zhai Fu

Sixty-two

Today is a particularly interesting day. We held a particularly interesting meeting called a planning meeting. Today, the children jointly decided on a plan for the year's work.

The children didn't quite understand this meeting at first. Yu'er said, "Today there's a chrysanthemum meeting at the school." Chunxiang said, "No, it's a chicken flower meeting." Mr. Zhu finally had to explain what a plan was. "Children! How many meals do you want to eat a day?" Ying'er said, "Three meals." Wang'er said, "I want to eat four meals." Mr. Zhu said, "Okay, Ying'er's eating plan is three meals a day; Yu'er's eating plan is four meals a day." Xiao San said, "I understand, is the planning meeting an eating meeting?" Mr. Zhu said, "Eating is an important thing, we must put eating in the plan. But what else do you have to do besides eating?" Qiu'er said, "Reading, writing." Lan Hua said, "; There's also sweeping the floor, cooking." Baozhu said, "Practicing boxing." Yang'er said, "Playing, sleeping." A'er said, "Peeing, pooping can also be considered important things, right?" Mr. Zhu said

: "They are important things, you must have a bowel movement every day. If you don't have a bowel movement for a day, you'll have nightmares at night, and you'll feel uncomfortable. Pooping is a very important thing." Everyone laughed. Mr. Zhu continued, "We write down all the things we do in a day, eating, reading, writing, sweeping the floor, cooking, practicing boxing, sleeping, playing, peeing, pooping, and when we do what, how many hours or how much of what we do, then it becomes a day's plan. Qiu'er - tell me your day's plan." Qiu'er said, "Three meals, two big bowls each meal, half an hour of planting, one hour of woodworking, one hour of Chinese, one hour of arithmetic, half an hour of writing, one hour of playing science tricks, half an hour of sweeping the house, one hour of practicing boxing, ten hours of sleeping, two hours of playing, one time pooping, peeing is uncertain." Mr. Zhu said, "This is Qiu'er's day's plan. Although he has left out many things, it is indeed a plan. A plan is to write down a list of the things we want to do so that we can see it often, so that we don't do this and forget that. We advocate what kind of life we live is what kind of education we receive: living a planned life is considered receiving a planned education: living an unplanned life is considered receiving an unplanned education. Speaking of plans: there is a plan for one day, a plan for one month, a plan for one year, a plan for three years, a plan for ten years, a plan for a lifetime, what we children should do in this year, how much each thing should be done, must be planned out, so that we are not rushed. Okay, let's make a year's plan for the ancient temple children."

The Shanghai Local Supplement of the Shen Bao

Opinion

Young Maids and the Class System 152

— Buddha

Yesterday's article in this publication, "The Pitiful Ah K," described the situation of an underage maid being seduced by the young master, and then being fired by the mistress upon discovery, who scolded her as "rotten goods." The maid could only leave in shame and tears. Such incidents are common in aristocratic families. This is an abstract way of putting it.

But such incidents are extremely unfair in terms of reason and justice. A pure and innocent young maid is clearly seduced by her son, yet instead of making her a member of the family or compensating her for the loss, she is fired and called "rotten goods." And on the maid's side, it's as if she shouldn't have tried to climb up to the young master, as if she, a lowly person, has committed an egregious crime that she ought to repent for. This kind of oppressed mentality and the harsh methods of capitalists are often like this.

As for the marriage system, although there are no class restrictions in law, in the minds of most corrupt people, the invisible class system is stricter than legal regulations. Officials must marry officials, and the wealthy must marry the wealthy in order to be considered "well-matched." Otherwise, they laugh at wealthy families for losing their status, or laugh at poor families for shamelessly climbing the social ladder.

In the Republic of China, all people are supposed to be equal. The so-called poverty and wealth are just distinctions between having money and not having money. Lowliness and nobility are just distinctions between being lucky and unlucky. What other differences are there? As for round heads and square feet, ears, eyes, noses, and everything else, they are the same. Why is it that a young maid cannot marry the young master, and the young master cannot marry the young maid?

I'll go a step further and say that wealthy families must marry poor families, and noble families must marry lowly families. If this were the case, then wealth, nobility, poverty, and lowliness could be evenly distributed. Those in poverty and lowliness would be endlessly grateful. If you are already wealthy and marry wealth, it is redundant. If you are already poor and marry poverty, it's like adding frost to snow. This is a bad habit of our country. If we don't break this bad habit first, the class system in society will never be eradicated!

Random Thoughts on the Early Spring of the 21st Year 153

— Xiao Chang

I resent the meddling spring breeze, blowing up the proud sun from the east sea. Fragrant grasses vainly grow green in the three paths, the delicate peach blossoms sadly illuminate a pond of red. I idly talk of Zhang Xu's palace willows, only Cai Yong cherishes the withered wutong trees. All day long, I sing sorrowful songs as a substitute for weeping, a white-haired old man bitterly chanting at the edge of the world.

Second Poem

Gazing far over the plains, the grasses are lush. Embroidered rivers and mountains are trampled by iron hooves. The cuckoo's mournful cries are heard in Hebei, the oriole's songs have no dreams of reaching western Liaoning. On the battlefield, I will pity the blooming flowers one day. In the bustling city, I now listen to ghostly wails. Where can I find the past of Taicheng? The green willow embankments are deeply locked in the smoke of war.

Third Poem

The Southern Dynasties were like a dream, vying for extravagance. Now I hate the past mistakes that cannot be redeemed. One must learn from the generals and be called a great tree, and not greedily watch famous flowers in Luoyang. At this time, thorns grow in the courtyard. In the past, brave soldiers were like claws and teeth. When the raging waves are stemmed by the collective effort, how many people will wander about, lamenting that they have no home?

Science

Methods for Cleaning Clothes 154

— Tan Guanhan

The hot weather easily causes people to produce sweat. If you are not diligent in cleaning, the sweat secreted from the skin will stick to the clothes, and an unpleasant odor will evaporate. No one welcomes this kind of odor, even oneself will feel uncomfortable. Secondly, clothes are worn on the body, so you can't use special care to protect them. During banquets, beside desks, or when it rains, on muddy roads, and so on, if you are not careful, you will inevitably get tea stains, meat juice, ink, paint, mud, paint, and other unexpected and unsightly stains. At that time, wouldn't you feel deeply unpleasant? Therefore, the method of cleaning clothes is probably something that readers would like to hear about.

Usually, the detergents for clothes are mostly soap, because the raw materials of soap are made of things like fat and sodium. When it encounters water, it emits fatty acid salts and alkali. The acidic salt is a smooth protobody that can help with washing. Alkali is a free protobody that can separate the dirt on the clothes and dissolve it in water.

However, although soap is the best detergent, there are a few things to pay attention to when using it. (1) Ordinary soaps sold on the market have different prices, but a cheap soap that costs twice as much cannot match the effectiveness of half a piece of expensive soap. The distinction between them is only two types: hard and soft. The former is a superior type, and the latter is an inferior type. (2) Washing clothes with soap seems very simple, but in fact, the water is also very important when washing. Using hot water is better than using cold water, because the washing effect of hot water is much stronger than cold water, which can make the soap liquid penetrate into the fibers of the clothes and easily remove dirt. (3) In the interior of the country - where there is no tap water, you must recognize the different degrees of hardness of the water. Rainwater, river water, and lake water are soft, and spring water, sea water, and well water are hard. Soap detergent is most suitable for soft water, otherwise, it will generate a kind of neutral sodium salt or potassium salt and calcium salt of fatty acid, which can reduce the washing effect.

Clothes that have been used for a long time often cannot be as white as new again, so you have to use a bleaching method. There are three types of bleaching agents, such as bleaching powder, chlorine white, and hydrogen peroxide, but usually bleaching powder is used. When using it, first soak the material to be bleached in cold water, then pour a spoonful of bleaching powder into half a basin of clean water, mix it evenly, and then take the clear bleaching liquid and pour it into the basin containing the clothes, and then soak the clothes again. After one hour, take it out, wring it dry, soak it in dilute hydrochloric acid for about half an hour, then take it out, wring it dry, soak it in sodium hyposulfite for about ten minutes, take it out, rinse it thoroughly with clean water, and after drying, it will return to its former glory. (Regarding the method of making bleaching powder, I will describe it in another article when I have time, but it is also available in pharmacies, so it is very easy to buy and use.)

Fashion 155

Modern Women and Umbrellas

Modern Youth and New Style Straw Hats

Text / Fan T

Suggestions from the Society for Improving Social Customs on Reforming Marriage Customs 156

— Xiao Kangshi

Marriage: is inevitable for everyone, and is one of the biggest problems in life, simply to seek happiness. However, our country's customs are extremely superficial and conventional, and the recent social trends have become even more extravagant. According to the current expenses of marriage, the poor need at least a thousand gold, as for the rich, it can be several thousands or even tens of thousands of gold. Their psychology embraces vanity and a desire to surpass others, showing off their glory with lavish scenes, but they do not investigate whether they can achieve true happiness. Therefore, the rich create the trend, and the poor follow suit, losing the true meaning of marriage as a pursuit of happiness, and instead suffering endless future troubles.

We see that the marriages of the poor in society, influenced by the trend of extravagance, have no choice but to drink poison to quench their thirst, whether it be selling their belongings, incurring debts, going bankrupt, or committing suicide due to economic pressure, they go to extremes. Alas! This kind of evil custom, under the current state of national decline and impoverishment, cannot be allowed to continue, and urgent reform should be sought quickly. Here are three aspects within my limited view, listed below.

(1) The Dowry Should Be Abolished. The most important thing in our country's marriage customs is the dowry, simply hoping for the praise of relatives and friends, and the compliments of neighbors, which is all meaningless. And the meaningless "lucky money" given to the moving workers also costs a lot. Therefore, in my humble opinion, the dowry should be abolished, and the furniture should be purchased by the man himself, which can save the arguments about the thickness of the dowry, and can also save a lot of unnecessary money.

(2) Reciprocal Congratulatory Gifts and Wedding Banquets Should Be Abolished. When relatives and friends have marriage matters, of course, they congratulate each other with money or gifts, and the host throws a large banquet. What is the meaning of this reciprocal socializing? The congratulator gives a congratulatory gift and gets a cup of wedding wine, and the host receives some gifts and invites the congratulators to eat wedding wine. Both gifts and wedding wine are wasted, with no real benefit. Therefore, in my humble opinion, it should be abolished. On the wedding day, some refreshments should be prepared to thank the relatives and friends who attended the ceremony, so that both parties will not spend money.

(3) Should Be Economical and Simple. According to today's living standards, all the expenses and ceremonies of marriage should be economical and simple, and the wasteful and superficial ones should be thoroughly abolished, seeking happiness in reality.

Are the above three points appropriate? I would also like to ask the wise to discuss it. However, worldly customs are difficult to break. We poor scholars sing loudly, but if there are no adults and gentlemen to promote it, what effect will it have? However, the bone is stuck in the throat, and I have to spit it out!

Discussion on Improvement 157

— Huanhua

Recently, the editor of this journal advocated a society for improving social customs, which is indeed in line with the needs of modern society and a major mission for newspapers.

However, the word "improvement" is a good thing to say, of course, it is to correct the malpractices of the deformed society and the imperfect society, and bring them back to the good track. However, in a vague sense, criminal improvement and illegal improvement are also called improvement. Such improvement, although the name is still improvement, actually changes the well-intentioned goodness.

Now let's take a few examples to talk about it: (1) Several newspapers in Shanghai are also singing loudly about improving society, among which some advocate improving women's fashionable dresses, which can cultivate women's psychology of extravagance and bad habits, and the resulting moral degradation, economic pressure, family changes, and other malpractices, are countless. Some also advocate improving cigarettes. From the industrial standpoint, it can be said that there is a need to promote benefits and eliminate harms. However, for the sake of smokers, it hinders development, damages the brain, and wastes money. Is it necessary to improve it? (2) The lethal weapons used to kill people in various countries are now actively researching and improving. What does this improvement mean? Japan is also actively researching and improving Manchukuo. What does this transformation mean? (3) There is a popular play on the stage called "Improving the New Killing of Sons." Killing sons and wanting to improve, this is truly a groundbreaking improvement. Extending this to the current society, cases of adultery, theft, and murder are constantly emerging, so why can't it be said to be improvement? Even the recent inhuman act of dogs copulating with humans is also the result of Chen Xin's improvement!

Therefore, anyone who wants to discuss improving society must try their best to stand on the side of good. When you think of a new problem and propose a new method, it must be able to bring real benefits to society, family, and individuals, and then it can be called improvement, and then it will not fail the hard work of the editor of this journal in setting up the society, and then it can make the depressed and hopeless people gain some welfare.

Let's try to base ourselves on the past arguments of this journal: it advocates science and improves technology to seek the popularization of industries with backward production. Exposing the inside story and punishing the people to seek the fundamental overthrow of the sinful society. Studying the evolution of social groups and family systems to adapt to the timely production of trends is a great mission. How great is this improvement, how beautiful and good is this, this is exactly the editor's hint to the readers of the discussion society, this is also a bright path for the readers of the discussion society. However, inferring other things from one instance is up to the readers' efforts.

Discussion on Improving Family Economy 158

— Ms. Ouyang Jinping

With a good economy, there is a good family. Otherwise, the husband will have a worrisome burden, the wife will sigh with skill, and the children will cry for food. The environment is forced, and there is no peace. Therefore, the family economy must be carefully studied. Moreover, in this era of rice as pearls and firewood as cassia, if we do not know how to improve the economy, how can the family be prosperous? Here are some of my views, written below.

Hold a family affairs meeting every year to discuss economic issues.

Allocate the income of salary and wages in a complete way. For example, if the annual income is one thousand yuan, then allocate it as follows.

A. Food expenses account for two-tenths

B. Room rent expenses account for two-tenths

C. Clothing expenses account for one-tenth

D. Self-study and entertainment expenses account for one-twentieth

E. Miscellaneous and pocket money (for furniture, medical treatment, condolences, etc.) account for one-tenth

F. Education expenses account for one and a half-tenths

G. Savings expenses account for two-tenths

And order family members to pay attention to the rules of thrift.

(1) Men and women in the family should work together and not sit idly, in order to save the cost of employing servants.

(2) If the clothes are not damaged, it is not appropriate to sew new clothes again. The remaining money should be saved for interest, or to prevent accidents and increase room rent.

(3) Do not set foot in entertainment venues on non-holiday rest days, so as to avoid excessive spending.

(4) Do not spend a penny on superstitious trivialities.

(5) Charitable donations should be donated as much as possible with the accumulated interest from the savings item.

(6) Old and young in the family should abstain from smoking and drinking to save unnecessary expenses.

Market News 159

The New Invention of 320-Needle Cicada Wing Stockings. Mr. Yu Zhijing, a pioneer in the Shanghai hosiery industry, has returned to Shanghai after practicing machinery in Germany. He has invented a 320-needle men's silk stocking, named Cicada Wing Stocking. Because this stocking is thick and thin, wearing it is like cicada wings, so it is cool and comfortable, most suitable for summer weather. It is now on sale. Exclusive sales locations: Nanyang, Dadong, Xiaodongmen, Yong'an, Dadong on Nanjing Road, Guang Shengxiang on Sanma Road, Nanyang on Wuma Road.

Family Weekly Issue 12 Published. Family Weekly Issue 12, published by the Family Weekly Editorial Department at 24 Jia, Yuanmingyuan Road, Shanghai, has now been published. The content is rich and worth reading.

The Postal Workers' Peking Opera Troupe is Reorganized. The Shanghai Postal Workers' Peking Opera Troupe has been famous in Shanghai since its establishment and has been around for many years. Due to the January 28th Incident, the troupe was located in Zhabei, which was in the line of fire, resulting in its suspension. Now that the situation has been calmed, the association has rented a house at 230 Laobazi Road as a club, so the troupe has moved in and is being reorganized.

The Vocational Guidance Center Seeks Talents. The Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center was entrusted yesterday by a rural primary school in Zhejiang to hire a principal, with a graduate of a rural normal school, rich in agricultural knowledge, had served as a rural school teacher, able to endure hardship, and have the skills of a farmer, as qualified, with a monthly salary of forty-five yuan. A primary school in Zhejiang entrusted to hire a senior grade teacher, who must be from Jiangnan or the west-central Zhejiang area, graduated from a old-style normal school, or have a considerable level, proficient in Mandarin and English, and skilled in art work, understand child psychology, and be diligent and able to endure hardship, as qualified, with a monthly salary of thirty yuan. A company in this city entrusted to hire a female clerk, who must be able to speak English, be familiar with the situation of various girls' schools, and have social skills, as qualified, with a monthly salary of thirty yuan. A foreign firm entrusted to recruit four lighter salesmen, with generous commissions. If anyone is willing to take the above positions, they can go to 80 Hualong Road to discuss in person with the center.

Hamburger Ink Firm Adds Retail Department. The "Military Officer Brand" ink issued by the Hamburg Ink Firm on Xishang Lin Street, Wuma Road, this city, is of excellent quality and low price. It has always been exclusively engaged in large-volume wholesale in other cities. It is recently heard that the firm, in view of the increasingly developed printing industry in this city and the increasing demand, has specially added a retail department, so that the printing industry in this city can also enjoy the firm's exquisite ink. Now is the autumn discount period, the firm has specially sold each item at a particularly low price, and also has Victory Factory exquisite ivory cigarette holders as gifts for customers.
